What can make them return is the heavenly content, the power of original conscience. It is not the conscience you currently possess, but the power of original conscience. If you cannot find the feeling that bursts forth from the power of original conscience and original heart in your faith journey, you cannot go to heaven. You cannot stand as a child of God.

The way to repay the enemy
Repaying God's enemy is not done by stabbing with a spear. How should it be repaid? You must clarify Satan before God, the Absolute Being. When you say, "God, is it not like this and that?" God must be able to respond, "Yes, yes." You must completely accuse and strike down Satan. Satan is the thief of the heart.

So why has Satan become God's great enemy? From the day he took humanity away, he became the great enemy, and what is the content of that enmity? It is that he took away the heavenly love connection that God wanted to establish with the ancestors of humanity through the ideal of creation. Therefore, he is the great enemy. He is the great enemy. Now we have come to know this fact.

Satan's work begins from within my body. Therefore, I must conquer my body. When I think of this, it is not a problem to be hungry, naked, or insulted. It is not a problem to be imprisoned in a cage.

You must repay the enemy before you die. You must repay the enemy before you die. You must die after repaying the enemy. The enemies of the True Parents, the enemies of the True Bride and True Bridegroom, and the enemies of the True Children remain on heaven and earth, and it is the responsibility of Christianity to eradicate these enemies.

To eradicate the enemy, you must evoke God's heart. To evoke God's heart, you must understand God's inner circumstances. You must know what you did not know.

You must know that God, who created Adam and Eve and rejoiced so much, was so sorrowful when Adam and Eve fell. You must know that God fought for thousands of years centered on Abel and Cain, centered on Noah, centered on Abraham, Moses, and Jesus.

When you come to know such a Father, your heart will burst forth. You must be shocked. You must be deeply shocked. You must receive an impression that you have never felt from any preacher or teacher in the world. You must be able to testify to the emotional connections historically, contemporarily, and futuristically in order to live. 

Therefore, you must repay the enemy. You must repay God's great enemy. This land is a land where good people have shed blood. It is a land that has shed blood because of the enemy.

God's heart, which raises you in place of Himself, is pitiful. Why must humanity go through this path to atone for the betrayal of heaven? Since the circumstances have become this way, to resolve it, you must take the opposite path.

Have you ever wept several times longing for your Father? Have you searched for the place where your lost Father is crying out, not caring if your legs are broken, struggling through mountains and fields? There must be a place where your Father is longing for you and crying out; where could that place be? Have you ever wandered in search of that place?

Today, we have stepped forward with absolute content before the world, before the entire universe, but what do we know? We know that God is my Father and what the heart of the Father is like. Therefore, now, the Father created humanity to see the appearance of dutiful sons and daughters, so why is there sorrow? Why is there lamentation? Why is there hardship? All of this is our sin for not being true sons and daughters.

We must become a group that cries out, "Father!" in lamentation. Only then can we return. Only then can we return. Only then can we become new.

We have lost everything. We have nothing. I myself have nothing. I do not desire honor. I do not desire to become your teacher. I only pray to die in a place where I will not leave regrets, saying, "I should have done this a bit more in place of the Father before I fell."

When lonely groups are placed before us, heaven is in pain. Something that cannot be suppressed is bursting forth from the heart. We have turned away from worldly connections and returned to heavenly feelings. Since we have turned back, we should not go with a spirit of despair but should go with strength.

Heaven has waited for thousands of years. Even now, He is waiting. Even if we walk through the valley of death, He is waiting. Whenever you go out and struggle, heaven is waiting. The person who is shouting here knows this well. I thought it was the end, but I have come to know that it is not the end. I thought I would fall into despair, but I have come to know that heaven exists.

Now you must become a group that holds onto the True Parents and cries out, a group that holds onto the arms of the Father who has struggled to find the True Parents and cries out. Thus, you must become true children who are established before the True Parents and at the same time long for true siblings. This is the content you must prepare.

Humanity must long for God, who is the vertical Parent, and must establish the way of filial piety before Him. However, we are those who have not resolved the sorrow of the Fall. What is a dutiful child? You know the parable of the prodigal son, right? If there is a brother who can run out to the returning prodigal son with the heart of a father who waits for the prodigal son with tears in his eyes, the father will give him the entire inheritance.

A way to eradicate God's great enemy
Today we have come to know. We have come to know that the prodigals of the world are also our blood relatives. History has flowed, but in His heart, He cannot forget the sons and daughters of death, and even after going through six thousand years of hardship, He cannot let them go. The heart and resentment of the Father remain with them.

When facing heaven, you must have the heart of a parent whose overwhelming feelings bring tears to their eyes. Burn with such feelings. If there is someone carrying a burden in the sweltering heat, hold onto them and cry out to feel the heart of the Father and the heart of the Mother. What they are laboring for is for me, so try to say, "I will carry the burden." Block the path and, with a heart of longing, cry out, "Brother! There is a path left to go, but where are you going?" If you have such feelings, heaven will be with you on your path.

The person speaking here also had no companions. I have walked a lonely path. My heart is filled with sorrow, anger, and deep resentment. However, I feel that it cannot compare to the labor of heaven, and I cannot stand before God, who has come out with resentment for six thousand years. Yet, I also know that whenever I feel inadequate to bear the responsibility I have taken on, heaven holds me and encourages me. Become a son or daughter who can be welcomed by God, who comes to you even when others flee. You must know that God is waiting for you in such a place.

When Jesus was to be crucified, the disciples fled in fear of the cross. However, even if he was a thief, when he thought sorrowfully of Jesus’ situation as he was dying, and was filled with the desire to touch and feel Jesus’ body, that thief was saved. The blood kinship of heaven begins from here. It cannot be done with words. There are many who speak. There are thousands and tens of thousands of means and methods. However, the greatest truth of all truths is the heart of love. In the heart of love, there can be no means or methods. We must know that this is the only way to eradicate God's great enemy.

If there is someone who holds onto God and receives God's heart and feelings to confront Satan, no one can even open their mouth before them. When humanity does not know God, Satan can play with humanity as he pleases and dominate them, but when one appears with the content that arises through heavenly feelings, even countless Satans will surrender. Therefore, whether I die or live, it is Father. This blood, though received from Satan, must be transformed and gathered as the blood of the Father, and I must long for that place. Only then will Satan fall.

Our responsibility
Now we must pray. Is your blood and flesh currently belonging to Satan? When your blood is shed and your flesh falls, you must pray not to become one who will be taken by Satan, crying, "Oh, my blood! My flesh!" When you fall, vomiting blood, you must be someone whom the Father can hold and weep for.

Until now, countless people have come and gone on this earth. Many people live on this earth today. Countless people are searching for the way of virtue, but to this day, they have not met such sons and daughters. Even if Peter was hung upside down on the cross, he could not be held by God because he had the sin of betrayal against Jesus. Countless people have disappeared like dew in the execution grounds, but because of the sin of betraying the only begotten son sent by God, while that death could be acknowledged as a condition for indemnity, it could not be recognized as having shed good blood and flesh for God.

You see, thirty million people are struggling without knowing which way to go. Therefore, you must become leaders before this starving nation. You must go forth with the iron rod of life, breaking the iron net of death before the nation that is crying out and sweating in the world of death, shouting, "Comrade! Brother! I am here!" Thus, by establishing the connection of father and son, and the connection of brothers, forming tribes and nations, the day will come when the heavenly people will emerge, the sovereignty of heaven will be restored, and the resentment of heavenly feelings will be resolved. You must clearly understand this.

Do you feel sorry for the clothes you are wearing? Let them go. Do you have treasures? Throw them into the air.

You must know that these become bait for Satan in approaching heaven. If there are those who do not care about shedding tears of blood for goodness and are sleepless to provide even a single inch of land or a single piece of clothing, that nation will dominate the world.

Heaven is looking for such people. Even if a person weeps until their eyes are swollen with longing for the Father, even if they go mad, that person will not go to hell. Even if they collapse while starving and being pointed at and mocked by many people, if they collapse while longing for the Father, that place will not become a vacant lot.

Today, we have stepped forward to create an era. We have emerged as new pioneers in the revolutionary path of heavenly providence. Therefore, the blood of pioneering must pulse in our bodies, and the flesh of pioneering must pulse as well. We must hold onto this sleeping nation and pray toward heaven, and we must struggle to become the comforters of this starving nation. If you become such people, even if you are trampled and pushed down in this era, the day will surely come when you are needed before this nation and before humanity.

We long for such groups. We long for such families. We must sacrifice everything to gather such people. Thus, we must explain the parents to those who do not know their parents, and to those who do not know the connection of brothers, we must break the conventional wisdom and let them know the true connection of brothers that transcends the boundaries of the spirit world and the physical world. Thus, if your hunger means I cannot eat, and when I eat, you must eat too, if that heart becomes stronger than the national sentiment and any ideology or doctrine in the world, then you must clearly understand that God's work of resolving resentment will unfold automatically.

I feel a sense of resentment when I hear that you were scolded when you went out to evangelize, but in my heart, I rejoice and pray. Why? Because that person has returned with a heart that has formed a deep connection with the heart of heaven, not with human feelings. There will be a day to boast about that before heaven.

Today, we, under a new determination, pouring out all our passion, carry the heavenly resentment in our bodies as one body and become a bomb that will explode in hell, shedding blood, and I believe that a tower of victory will be erected there.

Only when such groups emerge will the resolution of this nation unfold, and this nation will be able to move toward a new ideal, and centered on a global spirit, it will be able to lay the foundation for a new nation. You must thoroughly feel that this standard will become a shield of victory that can eternally resolve God's resentment.

<Prayer> Father, when I think of the 40 peaks that have passed, from a human perspective, it is tiresome. The passing of sorrowful days is the inevitability of history, and we have come to know that our actions on this earth are also the heavenly path to resolve the twists and turns of the fallen world.

The way to repay God's great enemy is to become a parent in a land without parents, to become a brother in a land without brothers, and to become a heavenly people in this universe without heavenly people. Therefore, we have cut off all connections to worldly parents and all connections to worldly couples.

As the time has come for a new heavenly emotional connection to take root on this earth, we see that today's trends are actively swept in that direction. Today, as heaven seeks a region where the center of heart from heaven is rooted on earth, there must be such a place for the heavenly will to be fulfilled, and we also know that the day will surely come when we will resolve heaven's resentment and raise the flag of victory before all people.

Therefore, when I think of this movement that seeks to find the foundation of such heart on this lonely Korean Peninsula, among the people who have fallen and bled, I am deeply grateful, Father.

Now, we must convey the new words of life before this dying nation, and we must share the twists and turns tangled in tears of blood. So that many lives may be newly revived, though this nation and this world are in the autumn season, may they be equipped with the energy of spring centered on the new words. Thus, may we fulfill the history that can transition to a new world that can look toward the summer season and the new autumn season. Father, I earnestly wish and hope that You will be with the footsteps of those who go forth with hearts filled with tears of blood.

Having completed the entrusted 40-day journey, may we meet again, holding hands and opening our hearts, sharing tears for the nation and speaking of the sorrowful and resentful facts, and if there are any grievances, may we say, "Father!" and rather bless the nation, allowing them to return with the evidence that they loved this nation in their hearts.

Though I do not wish to send them on a difficult path, this is the heart of the one responsible, but because there are still twists and turns in heaven, I cannot help but send them that way, and I know that path is the inevitable course we must take. 

Therefore, may they offer all their sincerity to present even a drop of blood before the Father, to present even a piece of flesh before the Father, and to take one action for the Father, and if there are any wrongs, may You forgive them.
Please, embrace them and protect them, I earnestly hope and pray for this.  
The path of tracing the heart is a lonely path, a sorrowful path, a path of tears,  
so I earnestly hope that You, Father, will personally comfort and bless us. Whether we live or die, let us hold on to Heaven, and may we become sons and daughters who can give glory to the Father until the day we fall.  
I earnestly hope and wish that we can continue our march until the day we can present Heaven and Earth in Your embrace and make our enemies submit. I earnestly request that You be with us until we can sing the glory of a groundbreaking victory by mobilizing the heavenly and earthly conscientious people in this march. In the name of the Lord, I have prayed. Amen. *  
5)  
Have a New Resolve  
<Summary of the Message> Our principle is the word obtained through sweat, tears, and blood. Therefore, let us become sons and daughters who can invest all our blood and flesh to embrace the world and the universe and approach the Father.  
We must walk the path of tears for the day of glory. The sweat, tears, and blood shed for goodness will never be in vain. We must keep going, and no matter how much we do, it is never enough. Let us forget all past matters.  
Now we must fight for our brothers. When the final end time comes, we must cut off our attachment to the world. At that time, there will be a great judgment, which includes the first judgment of the word, the second judgment of character, and the third judgment of heart. We must pass through all of these.  
Now is not the time to focus solely on individuals. We must unite our individuals, nations, and the world, and even the spiritual world to fulfill the ideal of creation.  
Therefore, those who walk the path of the way must transcend the concepts of nation and state.  
Those who live with the theme of love are Christians without nationality. Thus, all Christians are one brotherhood united in love, the people of Heaven.  
Now is the time to seek the citizens of Heaven. The time of blind faith has passed. Let us once again critique ourselves from that perspective.  
August 31, 1960 (Wed) night, former headquarters church.  
* This message was given to the members who returned after completing the second summer 40-day evangelism, and it has been organized from what was published in <Seonghwa> No. 1 (after registration with the Ministry of Culture; dated October 12, 1970).  
In the world of heart, the value of the individual and the whole is the same. What remains in history is not human feelings but heavenly feelings. Becoming the bride of Heaven is not an easy task. No matter how devoted a filial son, loyal minister, or virtuous woman may be, they cannot surpass a person who knows God's heart at the end.  
God has labored for 6,000 years to establish one truth on this earth. During that time, He could not express all the words He wanted to say. When the voice saying "My son" is heard on this earth from such a God, the judgment on this earth will end.  
He is a pitiful and wronged God who has cried infinitely and has been unjustly struck. Jesus came as the Messiah of the word, reality, and heart, but due to the disbelief of the Jewish people, He could not fully fulfill His role as the Messiah and must come again. The time for His return has now come.  
Let us abandon the fallen nature of pride, jealousy, anger, and stubbornness and become those who inherit the Father's legacy of sorrow, pain, and injustice. Those who work diligently with sincere heart and shed tears will not fall. Until now, we have come out for ourselves, but from now on, we must move forward for the nation and the world. To do this, we must shed more sweat, tears, and blood. Let us make a new resolve and oath. Let us have a sincere heart toward Heaven.  
Let us be those who shed sweat for the earth, tears for the nation and humanity, and blood for Heaven. My body and mind are not mine but belong to the Father, so let us dedicate our bodies and minds entirely for this nation and humanity, which have no place to rely on and nothing to trust. *  
6)  
Show Greater Attachment  
<Summary of the Message> Now is the time when all humans are losing their attachment to democracy, communism, and any ideology. Furthermore, humans are even losing their attachment to themselves. The situation in Korea is also the same. Those engaged in the four professions (scholars, farmers, artisans, and merchants) are all losing their attachment to their occupations. Therefore, the biggest issue is to rekindle this attachment.  
We only need to show them a greater attachment than they have ever had to anything. This ultimately leads to the issue of heart for the purpose.  
When we show a greater attachment to their lives than they have for themselves, they will develop an attachment to eternal life. *  
September 2, 1960 (Fri), former headquarters church.  
* This message was given in response to the suggestions of those who served as evangelists during the first 40-day summer evangelism period of the first seven-year course, and it has been organized from what was recorded by former association president Yoo Hyo-won in his notebook, with the title added for convenience by the editor.  
7)  
Direction of Providence and the Words of the New Era  
<Summary of the Message> Heaven has brought about history from the place of being trampled. All cultures have emerged through the trampled masses, transitioning from individuals to nations and states.  
Now is the time to let go of each one's attachment. All paths have emerged from cutting off attachment to oneself. Heaven also drives all humans to lose their attachments. One cannot establish heavenly things while being attached to worldly things. This is the end time.  
The present world flows in a direction that causes both democrats and communists to lose their attachments. Religious people and those of the way will also be like this. Therefore, religions will become more divided and abandon their sects. This is to eliminate evil for the sake of good.  
Thus, we are driven to the point of losing even our attachment to ourselves, reaching the point where it must be Heaven or nothing.  
In judgment, there is the judgment of the word, the judgment of the heart, and the judgment of character.  
Since Jesus, judgment has been based on whether one believes or does not believe in the word. Due to the fall, we have not been able to find the reality of truth, so we must establish a heartistic connection to find that reality.  
The word must be able to revive from the individual to the universe. Therefore, the word must transcend the universe. The words of Jesus in the Bible were spoken while He remained single.  
Those of the way are people without a nation. They must be able to establish a nation based on the ideology of the way. The ideologies of the way may differ, but there must be a point of convergence. Jesus established this through love.  
The ultimate purpose of judgment is not in the individual but in the whole. Therefore, the purpose of the word is in the cosmic.  
Until now, believers have not been able to establish a brotherly connection. Today's religions have not achieved such a purpose.  
Now, making people let go of their attachments is to help them abandon their past attachments and develop new ones. Humans have a heart that wants to devote themselves and have faith and attachment.  
Now, we need words that can evoke new attachments. These words must be able to help us step on our egos and rise. Furthermore, these words must be the words of cosmicism that emerge through heartistic connections.  
What can remain after clearing the entirety of history? It is only the heart. In matters of heart, it transcends the value of the individual or the whole. Thus, we possess God.  
History has sought a heart in which humans can feel at ease. When He says to love me more than anyone else, it is to help us find the ultimate place of the heart. The purpose of history is to find and bless the children of the heart.  
The heart of a parent loving a child is not two but one. If it is not a word that ignites the heavenly heart, then it must also be abandoned.  
As long as the Father's tears, blood, and sweat remain on this earth, we must return this. The cries of the heart between parents and children must fill this earth. The Messiah is the Messiah of the word, heart, and reality.  
Jesus could not complete the word and left.  
A movement of words that can evoke new attachments must arise. It demands blood for Heaven, tears for humanity, and sweat for the earth. Therefore, we must shed the blood of the heart, the tears of the heart, and the sweat of the heart. *  
8)  
The New World Coming  
Revelation 21:1  
<Summary of the Message> God's purpose of creation is to establish a theocentric humanism. As humans move toward Heaven, democracy also establishes the ideology of theocentrism.  
God governs the hearts of humans, and those humans govern the earth. For there to be a new world where heavenly feelings and human feelings can become one, there must be a suitable land and a new ideology.  
All newness must begin from the renewal of the heart. The issue is not a revolution of consciousness, but the issue is a revolution of conscience, and an even greater issue is a revolution of heart.  
We must establish a conscience motivated by God. Because we fell from the incomplete period, we have lost the heart standard to face God from the standard of completion.  
Until now, religions have not been able to cause a revolution of people's consciences and establish them in an absolute position.  
The suffering of humanity lies in the inability to rejoice while holding onto Heaven, humanity, and the earth.  
Those who cannot feel joy from nature are not of the way.  
To overcome the heart of hatred, the question is whether there is a greater power that can transcend it.  
A completed human is one who can embrace themselves, humanity, and God.  
September 11, 1960 (Sun) afternoon, former headquarters church.  
* This summary of the message has been organized from what former association president Yoo Hyo-won wrote down during his life.  
True admonition from someone who truly loves you is never forgotten. If there is admonition from the absolute love's subject, it will never be forgotten. Therefore, the time must come to receive the admonition and command of the Absolute. Christianity seeks such a person.  
Heaven, earth, and humanity must be bound together with God's heart. What makes a parent a parent? Is it the outer form or knowledge? It is the heart that makes one a parent. The same goes for spouses. If a couple is formed based on external conditions, it will break along with those external conditions.  
The reason a Christian does not care about death is that they have a heartistic connection with Heaven. A parent can die in place of a child because of such a heart.  
A true heart is moved toward God. The reason Jesus said to love me more than anyone else is that it is about having a heart that must relate to God.  
To stand before the true master, we must shed sweat for the earth, tears for humanity, and blood for Heaven. The new world can be realized when it starts from one word, raises the heart, and calls forth the heart to establish a global form.  
There is a need for an earthly movement where God can reign.  
There cannot be a religion centered around oneself. Therefore, one must be able to give the benefits of their salvation to the nation and the world. A religion centered on the individual will perish.  
We must raise a heavenly movement with an ideology that can unite Heaven, earth, and humanity.  
If humanity had not fallen, Adamism would become worldism. Thus, Jesus also brought Adamism. *  
9)  
The True Father and Children  
John 14:1-6  
<Prayer> History may have passed, but at this time, we hope to encounter and engage with the humble form of Jesus who will soon be crucified before the nation. How much sorrow, anger, loneliness, and injustice must He have felt? Among the chosen people of Israel at that time, many claimed to serve Heaven, but there was no one who knelt before Jesus, who was walking the final path of death, and shed tears while holding onto the hem of His garment. We know this heartbreaking fact.  
On that sorrowful day, countless ignorant people on the earth, as well as the chosen people of Israel, whom You have woven through 4,000 years of bloody history, did not know that the resentment that could not be resolved even with their wailing was bound in that one hour. Instead, they drove Jesus away with a heart of injustice, and we earnestly hope that we may realize that there is a realistic struggle that must be resolved, even if it means dying a million times, to address this deep-seated resentment that pierces our bones and flesh.  
He came for them, but they struck Him and crucified Him. They are a group that cannot be forgiven before the heavenly principle, a group deserving to enter the unquenchable sulfuric fire of hell. Yet, we are in a position where we cannot dare lift our heads before the Father, who has worked hard to find and establish the remaining people who have passed through the path of suffering and the cross and the continuous history of blood through the ages and centuries.  
We have come to realize that in seeking Heaven, we cannot boast of our own appearances, and those who wish to be loyal to Heaven must abandon everything, sacrifice everything, and forget themselves. Who have we gathered here for? Let us not be those who believe for our own sake.  
When we place the two characters of faith before us, we must understand that the purpose is not for ourselves but for the Father, for the Lord, and for the nation and Heaven and Earth. In the past, we believed for our own salvation, but now let us believe for the greater salvation history of the universe. Jesus fought with such a heart throughout His life, lived with the Father, and spoke with the Father, and may we not forget this.  
Today, we are in a rapidly changing and chaotic era heading toward a historical conclusion, but we wish our center to be dedicated to the Father. We desire to offer all that we have to the Father, but we cannot help but worry that we may not be worthy of receiving it.  
On this day, confessing our shortcomings before the Father, we have gathered longing for the Father’s merciful touch, the heart of love, and the embrace of the Father. May we feel the infinite love of the Father that we have never experienced on this earth during this one hour, and may we be able to sing the Father’s will forever while embracing Him and praising our connection with the Father.  
Many multitudes have bowed their heads before the Father, but what can I say? More than many words, may only the heart that can deepen our connection with You arise. May we repent of our past and realize our present shortcomings, longing for the original nature that the Father seeks and wishes to establish, and may a fervent revolution of the heart arise that can cry out toward Heaven.  
May the hearts of the messenger and the recipient become one. Let us not come to this place with anything from the world, and may this time be one where we can return to the heart of a child, allowing our bones and flesh to be reshaped in the grace of the Father.  
At this time, we believe that You know that lonely members have gathered from all over South Korea to pour out their sorrowful hearts before the Father, so at this time, may they...
Please grant us the same grace. Also, I believe that you know that countless brothers across the sea are being persecuted and going through trials at this time, worrying and being anxious for your will, so please protect them. We, who fight based on your will, earnestly hope and desire to be united as one heart, one mind, and one family until we become victors before you, Father. We ask that you oversee everything, and we request that you establish our entirety as yours. I pray all these words in your name. Amen.

<Word> The title of the message I would like to share with you is "The True Father and His Children." I will speak on this topic of the True Father and His Children. 

God's providence of salvation to establish the truth on this earth
Nothing that exists on this earth has not begun from the truth. Everything created through God's hands, based on the true foundation, is true. Since all that exists is true, the purpose of the existence of this universe must also be true. Before the true Creator, who created the true world of existence, all creations must exist as true beings forever. However, while the Creator remains as the true being, all creations that were made have lost the value of truth. This is an undeniable fact historically and environmentally. Since it began from the truth, the world must eternally sing the value of that truth. If such a world existed, there would be nothing in any aspect of our lives today that is not connected to the truth. However, since our lives are not like that, there is nothing more sorrowful and worrisome than this.

Before the subject of truth, centered around the value of truth, transcending time to forever boast of its own existence, even if there are differences between the whole and the individual, if there were a world where no differences could be found in value, we cannot deny the fact that all beings today would have no choice but to remain in a happy place. 

However, the world where the most true being, the most true Lord exists, remains only as our hope. Therefore, our life journey must lead us to seek that world again and return to the most true being. 

So, what is the truth? The truth cannot have an end from the day it began. As long as it exists, the truth shines beyond time and space for eternity. However, today we have never encountered or felt such a value of truth. 

If the Creator exists, He will work to restore humanity to the world of true goodness, where humans can enjoy the value of truth eternally in their living environment. This is the providence of salvation, the will of God who sends the Savior to save all of humanity. 

Truth itself is true existence, and all phenomena or actions that manifest it are also true. You cannot deny that we humans have a consciousness of existence. If we were to become true humans with this consciousness of existence, we would have no reason to lament. 

So, what gives rise to lamentation? When we hope for the highest purpose and the highest value, but that hope is not fulfilled in our living environment, sadness and pain arise. If we had established a standard of truth that could overcome such pain, a standard of truth that could push away any suffering, from that place our lives would have begun, and the two characters of pain would hold no power. Before the established value of the true heavenly principle, pain cannot show any power. Today, we are searching for the truth, yet we are unable to live with it because humanity has fallen. 

Then, if we ourselves are searching for the truth in our social environment, what kind of truth are we looking for? We are looking for the truth of the body. Furthermore, we are seeking the truth of the heart. Our body and heart are seeking true connections because they have the potential to connect with a greater cosmic ideal. We are searching for a true environment and a true universe. 

Before I can be true, I cannot perceive what is true. No matter how true the other party may appear, unless I possess even a small essence that can be true, I cannot comprehend it. Therefore, we are striving to establish our conscience and align it with the direction of humanity and morality to seek the truth. This is the historical reality. 

When my heart stands in a true position capable of perceiving the truth and my body lives centered on the truth in the living environment, from there, the truth can connect with me, connect with the environment through me, and connect with this earth and heaven. 

The path to finding the truth through all things and substance
When you reflect on yourselves, you will acknowledge that your body is not true and that your heart is not true. Then, what do we need? We need something that can prove the body as true and something that can prove the heart as true. This cannot be resolved within myself. If the relative standard of truth does not manifest, I cannot clarify the truth of my body or the truth of my heart. <Message> The title of the message I wish to share with you at this time is "Finding the True Foundation." I will speak briefly with this title. 

God must have established the creation of heaven and earth based on an unchanging foundation that cannot be altered. Humans were created with a purpose, and all things were created with a purpose, which we cannot deny. 

If we, who were created under such a purpose, do not have a solid foundation that cannot be altered in our hearts, bodies, lives, or ideologies, we must acknowledge that we are in a state where no one can move. 

The person who must become the true foundation must stand on an unchanging foundation that cannot be altered. However, when we reflect on ourselves today, we cannot deny that we are not standing on such an immutable foundation in our lives, bodies, hearts, and even our emotions. 

We are all in a state of lacking an unchanging foundation. If the absolute God created beings centered on a certain purpose, then those created beings must also have an unchanging foundation that cannot be altered under that purpose. However, if we are not in such a state today, it proves that we possess a fallen nature. 

The purpose that God intended to achieve, the unchanging heavenly foundation, has become estranged from humanity due to the fall. This is an undeniable fact. 

We often say that God is love. If God, who is love, loves the humans on this earth, is there anyone who possesses an unchanging foundation to receive that love? We also say that God is truth, but where is there a being equipped with a true foundation before the true God? 

We say that God is life and an unchanging ideology; is there anyone on this earth who possesses a foundation that can inherit that life and ideology? If we are asked this, we can only answer that there is none. 

No matter how well someone may be regarded or how much power they may have, if we were to open their hearts, there would not be a single person who could confidently stand as an object that can be an unchanging foundation before the absolute value, goodness, life, or circumstances that God desires. 

If there exists a Creator who is the essence of true life, true love, and true goodness, then He cannot help but think of destroying environments that lack such a foundation and creating any form of a true foundation or true platform. 

We must understand that this is the providence of salvation, and that religion emerged as a means and method to achieve that salvation.
Who should be the unchanging foundation that God, who created all things, can enjoy? It must be a person among all created beings. This is true when we consider life at its center, as well as when we consider God's unchanging love. It is a lament that a person, who should be the eternal foundation that cannot change before God, is not able to fulfill that role.

If we had become the unchanging foundation before God, who is absolute life and absolute love, there would be no unhappiness, no death, and no suffering. A being equipped with absolute conditions such as absolute life, absolute love, absolute ideology, and absolute goodness cannot be made to submit by anyone.

Conditions to Become a True Foundation
God must appear with absolute love, God must appear with absolute goodness, God must appear with absolute life and absolute ideology, and God must appear with absolute value before all created beings. Let us examine the stage of life we are living in now. People often want to assert themselves. We must not lose heart by looking at the twists and turns and myriad situations before us, but rather, we must look beyond this and see the Lord who longs to see us with compassion, and we must look upon God.  
My sorrow is not the issue. I can end my individual life, but the Father who carries the historical providence must go beyond my life and into the future, waiting for me with hundreds or thousands of times more earnestness than my desire to go. If we understand God's heart, who could possibly say they will not go?  
Let us comfort God. Let us comfort the God who has no eternal foundation. The pitiful image of Jesus, who is tormented without a foundation of heart, who, in the Garden of Gethsemane, faced the cold dew alone, clinging to the roots of the grass and weeping, who made Jesus into such a figure? All of humanity must realize that they are destined to stand together at the judgment seat of history and receive the atonement for their sins.  
Jesus hoped. He believed. He went on believing in those who nailed Him and drove Him away. He believed in the betraying disciples. Because there was a condition of belief, He could come back after the resurrection. One who has betrayed and become a traitor cannot be restored without atonement. This is how the heavenly order is. But how could Jesus go to find the betraying disciple? Even at Pilate's court, even at the moment of His end, He believed in Peter. He believed that Peter, who was dancing in the place of betrayal, was not that way. Even if He had to fall, because He believed Peter was not that way, after the resurrection, He could go to the disciples, and Satan could not oppose Him. We must understand that this belief became the motivation to lead the disciples to raise the flag at the forefront of the earthly restoration movement.  
Dear friends, dying is commonplace. We are destined to atone for and resolve this historical grudge. Even if we walk the path of death, we must resolve this. If we cannot eat, we must go on even if we have to starve; if we cannot wear clothes, we must go on even if we have to be naked; if we cannot sleep, we must go on even if we have to stay awake all night.  
We must not be indebted to others. If we are indebted, we must repay it with our blood and sweat and by cutting our flesh and bones. Only then can we establish the dignity of children who can communicate the heart of the heavenly order before Satan and become the victorious foundation that heaven desires. Do you know how much God longs for that foundation of victory? When we look at schools, societies, churches, any political party, any organization, we see that the foundation of victory is completely blocked.  
God waiting for humanity in a painful place  
How must the citizens of heaven, who are destined to walk the path of single-mindedness, walk this path? If we cannot go with wisdom, we must go with sweat and tears; if we cannot go with sweat and tears, we must go with blood. We must dedicate our sweat as God's sweat, our tears as God's tears, and our energy as God's energy. Blood must be shed for God, tears for humanity, and sweat for the earth. Thus, we must trample down the foundation of resentment that cannot allow God, the earth, and humanity to meet. This is what we must do. My emotional life is God's work and my work, and my work is the work of the earth and humanity. We must advance to the point where we can sing of the heavenly value centered around ourselves.  
Until now, history has been divided into heaven, religion, and earth. When we sought heaven, we found that humanity was lost, and when we sought humanity, we found that heaven and earth were lost. Now, through the heavenly heart, we must find it through our emotional life, which is the work of the Father, the work of the earth, and the work of humanity, and at the same time, we must feel it is our work. We must conclude with one ideological standard that has been unified from beginning to end, with the glorious victory in sight, and with our hands joined together,  
we are here to return what has been lost, so please accept it.  
We must be able to do this. God does not wish to meet such sons and daughters in heaven. He does not wish to meet in a luxurious place where all humanity gathers, nor does He wish to meet in the garden of happiness. He wants to meet on the foundation of bloodshed, in a complicated environment where tears must flow, and in the battlefield of struggle.  
Dear friends, you must understand this.  
Those who try to host the Father in glory cannot meet Him. In the place where blood and tears are shed, in the place where all people lose their center and are in confusion and chaos, in the place where life and death are intertwined, we must be able to say,  
Heaven, earth, humanity, my Father. Thus, the Father will say, "My son, you are the son I have longed for in heaven until now. You are the son I wanted to set before all people. You are my son whom I can boast of in heaven and on earth."  
We must receive the blessing of God. Only then will the true foundation I spoke of today, the true foundation of humanity, be realized.  
Through us, the point of happiness for heaven, earth, and humanity must appear on this land. This task must be shouldered by someone. If there is someone whose tears obscure their vision, who cannot walk and is crying out in despair, let them bury their head at the feet of those who can take responsibility and repent. If there are those who, despite being in a pitiful and desperate situation, do not think of their own bodies and go forward with a grateful heart for heaven and the will, shedding blood and sweat, then we must resolutely follow them.  
If such believers and conscientious people do not appear among this nation, especially among the youth of this nation, this nation will perish.  
I am the eternal and unchanging ideological foundation of God. Even if this appearance is poor, hungry, and lacking in everything, in heart, if I am not here, there is no one to hold Your hand; if I am not here, there is no one to adjust Your clothes; if I am not here, there is no one to fix Your shoes. Every part of You cannot be without me.  
On the day when those who can gather come together, we can conquer this satanic world without fighting.  
The important thing is ourselves. We must thoroughly understand that the problem is myself. We are brothers going for one purpose. We must recognize that it is not "I am I, and you are you," but rather "you are me, and I am you." We must be those who can look at our brother bleeding and collapsing on the battlefield and vow before heaven that we will shed our blood for him.  
We must do this even in places where we shed tears and sweat. Until the living foundation, the victorious foundation is established through your hearts, do not lose heart and go on. Then, I am confident that a great victory for the universe will surely come before you.  
<Prayer> Father, because You love us so much, You ask us to walk such a path, and we will go today and tomorrow. We will go even if we are sad, even if we are insulted, and even if we are trampled upon. Such great love, such great grace, that this Korea cannot repay in any way. With a heart asking how we can repay You, we bow our bodies, so please accept us according to Your will.  
Today, many lives are present here. Please grant us the conviction to step over and surpass this world of processes, knowing what position we are in. If we cannot do that, we must realize that we cannot disregard the future either, so let those gathered here today become the true foundation of God, even if it is just a part of their lives.  
Let us establish such a foundation in our body, heart, and spirit, and show it to this evil world, so that we can manage this evil world.  
In that place, let us give glory before the Father and be able to receive the praise of being Your sons and daughters, and I ask that You accept all of this. I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.  
12) A Place I Truly Want to Go  
Revelation 21:1-6  
The title I want to speak about today is "A Place I Truly Want to Go." I will briefly speak on this title.  
Humans and God Searching for a Better Place  
Countless humans living on this earth are wandering in search of a better place, even without knowing it. Just as humans living on this earth are like this, God, who is facing the earth, is also like this. If we acknowledge that the land we live on is not truly a good place, we cannot help but admit that we, who live in it, are also not true.  
If we acknowledge that we are not in a true world and not true ourselves, we cannot help but acknowledge that God, who deals with this world and us, is also not in His original form.  
In the historical process where God personally leads humanity, if God could have set humans in front of the unchanging foundation as beings that long for the true, then we humans could have stood in that true place. However, because God is not in such a place today, we humans can also be seen to be living in an unwanted place.  
In other words, humanity, in an imperfect state, is in a place longing for the true form.
Because of this, we must not forget that God, who has an inseparable bond with humanity, is in an unfair position where He cannot be in a perfect place alongside humans. 

Both heaven and earth are simultaneously longing for the true, and this is an undeniable fact whether we look at history or reality. The true place, the place we truly want to go, is not only longed for by us in reality but has also been yearned for by the prophets of the past who wove history, and it is a place that our descendants cannot help but long for as well. 

If God is truly love and the center of all things, then God has the responsibility to pioneer this imperfect human world, and we who live on earth must also move together under God's common goal to establish that true place we long for. 

If we have a conscience that aims for good, that conscience must operate under this purpose, and if there are religious organizations, they too must operate for that purpose. The true place we want to go, where we can enjoy with our hearts, in our lives, in society, and where all of humanity can enjoy, must be established in our life journey; otherwise, true happiness cannot exist for humanity, no matter how much history passes. Any ideology that claims happiness is impossible. 

As long as God exists, we must inevitably establish that true place where we can live joyfully on this earth. Until this is accomplished, wars on this earth cannot end, nor can all contradictory phenomena be eliminated. 

The goal of salvation aimed at rescuing such humans is collectively referred to as heaven in religious terms. Therefore, unless the restoration movement of heaven, as spoken of in religion, unfolds, we cannot go to that world we truly want to reach. If God exists, then that world must be achieved without fail. If God cannot fulfill the purpose of the promises made to humanity, then we do not need such a God. 

What kind of place is the true place we want to go? If God exists, this issue must be resolved, and if there are people following God, they must walk the path of destiny where they take on this task in their life journey. This world that is achieved in this way is called the ideal world. 

If humanity had not fallen, the phrase "the true place we want to go" would not be necessary. Because if humanity had not fallen, they would already be in that place. If humans had lived in such a world, the providence of restoration, or the providence of salvation, would not have been necessary for us. 

However, humanity has lost all of that. Therefore, countless heroes and martyrs who have come and gone until now have all started from a position of loss. All people of the past wanted to find that true place they long for, and they are still searching for it now, so we cannot deny that we are in a position of having lost everything. This is why we say that humanity has fallen. 

Due to the fall, the world of hope we desire has become irrelevant, and the world of ideals that should advance toward eternal existence has disappeared, becoming a world preoccupied with achieving physical ideals. We have lost the world of ideals that our hearts can hope for and rejoice in, that is, heaven. However, as long as the heart is active, we must inevitably establish the world that the heart aims for. 

So, if we say there is a true place we want to go, what kind of place is it? It is a place where we can meet God, the God we call upon. It is a world centered around true parents and true families, a world where true siblings live. Furthermore, it is a true nation centered around true people and true sovereignty. 

However, despite the countless people who have come and gone throughout history, there has been no one who has seen the true aspect of God, no one who has had true parents, no one who has had true siblings, and no nation with true kings and true sovereignty. That is why we are still searching for such things today. 

In this light, we find ourselves in a state where we have lost all the best ideological elements. Therefore, we must realize how pitiful our existence is. We must feel how pitiful we are living in such a reality. 

We must establish a standard that can turn our life journey in a new direction. No matter how happy someone claims to be in their current situation, that happiness cannot last forever. Every human being living on this earth, regardless of who they are, is undoubtedly a pitiful being. Of course, those who live pitifully in this world are pitiful, but it is time to realize that even those with great power and authority are also pitiful beings. 

Looking at the current situation in Korea today, everyone is bound by their lives. They are bound by social circumstances. They are in a position where they cannot resolve their issues no matter how hard they try. Despite their earnest hopes for tomorrow, they are bound by circumstances that prevent them from even thinking of solving such problems. This reality, which should lead me to eternal happiness, the true place I long for, is instead pulling me in the opposite direction. Here, there is fighting and suffering. 

Therefore, you may feel the need for friends to solve such an environment. Furthermore, you may wish for a leader who can pioneer such an environment. However, even if there are friends and leaders, if everything is not resolved, there arises a longing for a true brother who can solve such an environment through deep feelings. Not only brothers, but also a longing for true parents who can take responsibility for such an environment and embrace and love me cannot be avoided. 

So, are the friends you are dealing with in that environment true friends? Are the siblings you are dealing with in that environment true siblings? Are the parents you are dealing with in that environment true parents? No, they are not. They are not. 

Because it is an environment tangled by the ties of the fall, all the friends here are friends who cannot escape the ties of the fall, and the parents and siblings are the same. We are bound in such a position. 

If an ideal family centered on God, centered on original parents, and centered on original siblings were established in the true place we want to go, how happy would that be? However, having lost all such ideal conditions, we have become humans who must yearn for this and think about it conceptually, which is truly pitiful. The love of God is to save such pitiful humans. Because of this love, while humans on earth live in ignorance, entangled in the realm of death, God has been tirelessly working behind or in front of us to pioneer this path, and you must understand this fact. 

Every time you feel tired of this environment, you yearn for something new, and every time you dislike your position, you think of something new. However, this is not something you think of alone. Every time that happens, God is leading you to the world of original purpose behind or in front of you. You must recognize that God's hand is with you. 

This moment is a solemn time when God is opening the door of our hearts, which are pitiful and miserable in such an environment, and is shocking us to go to the true place. Therefore, we must recognize that this time is an important moment that cannot be missed in our lives. Through the new shock and feelings we receive at this time, we must analyze our past lives and criticize ourselves to move toward tomorrow as a new self. You will experience much of this through your personal life, family life, or social life. 

The issues that must be resolved 
God has been working throughout history to save humans in a pitiful position like orphans, coming from the perspective of a friend, a brother, a parent, and even a teacher. Yet, when that was not enough, He worked from the position of a servant. Even today, heaven is appearing before us as a savior, a parent, a brother, or a friend. 

The historical saints and great figures who have come to this earth and contributed to human history did not do so because they were inherently great. They were people sent by heaven to feel animosity toward the environment and evil, to criticize the times, and to present a new direction to the masses. 

Throughout history, our ancestors have never welcomed such people. Rather, they persecuted them and eventually drove them to death, as we well know. Therefore, no matter how proudly they walk around, even if they appear great, from God's perspective, they are a tribe of rebellion that cannot be tolerated. 

In your bodies, there remains the blood and flesh of ancestors who killed those who were sent by heaven, who revered heaven, and who lived for heaven. The ones who killed such people in the past are not the only traitors; those who betrayed heaven are not the only betrayers. We ourselves, who are connected by that blood and flesh today, are also in such a position. 

Heaven has not only worked in the historical process of the past but is also working in the reality you live in today. You may not know it, but heaven has come to you as a true friend at times. At times, it has come as a true brother, and at other times as a parent or teacher. However, we have not been able to recognize God as a friend, a brother, a parent, or a teacher. What greater sin could there be than this? 

Those who have been sent are not representatives of a single nation. They were sent by the Creator to represent the entire created world from heaven to earth, yet earthly humans have betrayed, persecuted, driven away, and killed such people, doing as they please. From this perspective, we are all beings who have received life through historical lineage, and therefore, without exception, we are all traitors and sinners who cannot be accepted before heaven. 

Where there is sin, there can be no happiness. Where there is sin, suffering follows, and due to the painful circumstances, it ends in destruction. Countless people living on this earth have not yet resolved the historical pain that seeps deeply into their hearts. They have not been able to remove the historical sorrow from their bodies. So how will we manage this historical despair, historical pain, historical sorrow, and the forces of historical death? How will we eliminate the forces of historical death that come through historical pain, and how will we remove this sorrow and suffering? 

Humanity must solve this problem. This is the urgent fate we face in this era. Therefore, we must gather our hearts, concentrate our sincerity, and devote ourselves to resolving it. Now is the time for that. It is time to reorganize the environment and, furthermore, to reorganize our hearts and minds. The issue is how to reorganize such a life centered on oneself. Humanity, moving toward the final gate of historical judgment, must resolve this power of death. Unless this problem is solved, even if there is a true place we want to go, that place will have nothing to do with us. Therefore, we must clear everything. 

God's greatest indignation 
We know that God exists and that there is also Satan, who is opposed to God. What kind of being is Satan? He is the greatest sinner among sinners in the historical process. He is the greatest sinner in history and its chief. For 6,000 years, Satan has opposed God, who has been working in providence. For 6,000 years, he has opposed God without fail, and even at this moment, he continues to oppose. 

No matter how evil humanity may be, they still think in their hearts of following heaven. They think of the true. However, Satan seeks to destroy even this human heart. Because Satan has opposed heaven's history, the entire world has become his stage, and even you have become a stage for Satan. 

So how can we subdue this Satan? We must clear away the sins of historical consciousness. We must remove the pain that has accumulated throughout history. It is not just the pain of the times that is the issue, but we must remove the historical pain. How can we expel this Satan from ourselves? We must be liberated from historical sorrow. Isn't that so? 

If there is something fearful in the world, there is nothing more fearful than Satan. No matter how fearful this era may be, it will eventually pass. However, since the day humanity fell, there has been one enemy that has not left humanity, and that is Satan, the devil, and the evil spirit. 

When we live on this earth, if there is an enemy, we can repay that enemy. If we cannot repay in this generation, we can repay through future generations. However, for 6,000 years, humanity has not been able to expel the enemy who has acted on behalf of God, nor has it ever repaid that enemy. The greatest indignation of God is that we have not been able to repay this enemy. 

What is the great judgment? It is not to annihilate humans on earth but to destroy the great enemy, Satan. This is the great judgment. It is to eliminate the historical enemy, the enemy of this era, and the enemy that can become an enemy in the future, which is Satan. 

Until now, Satan has tangled the path of saints who are trying to become true people, the path of those with true conscience. For example, let’s say there is a sovereign nation in this era. If one lives well or conscientiously under the constitution or ideology of that nation, they will be recognized as righteous. However, even if such goodness is recognized, as time passes, it can be overturned. When that happens, what was considered good in the past cannot be good today, and what is considered good today may not be good tomorrow. Isn't that so? The east cannot become the west, and the west cannot become the south. Such goodness is not absolute goodness. While temporary goodness may exist, absolute goodness cannot exist. 

To use a tree as an analogy, such goodness may correspond to the leaves, but it cannot correspond to the trunk or branches of goodness. Therefore, as the times change, the definitions of goodness and evil also change. The world after humanity's fall has become a world where standards fluctuate, leading to an indescribably tangled world. If God exists, He must either recognize this tangled world entirely as good, or break it all apart and recreate it, or completely cut it off and eliminate it; one of these three must happen. Without establishing one of these methods, it is impossible to lead this earth to a world of goodness.
The Problem at the End of Days
God does not judge people on earth as good or evil without any conditions. Of course, there is a difference between good people and evil people, but that difference is merely a matter of a blank sheet of paper. The standard of good is God, and the standard of evil is Satan. 

Humans are in a position where they can encounter both good and evil. So, how should this be resolved at the end of days? We must strike down Satan, the embodiment of evil. Only then will evil come to an end. Among the three methods mentioned earlier, what does it mean to strike down? It does not mean to strike down people. It means to strike down Satan, who is in opposition to the supreme good, God. If we can remove that Satan, humans will not be able to commit evil acts. Isn't that right? If the parents are good, their children will naturally be good as well. That is the law of heredity. If the parents are evil, their children will also be evil. When the root of evil is cut off and cannot act, evil will naturally be resolved.

As the end approaches, evil invades even our individual cells. Therefore, no matter how accomplished a person may be in the world, Satan occupies even that person's cells. Everything they do, including eating and living, is under the control of Satan. It is within that authority that today's world operates. However, on the other hand, the good centered on God is also emerging. Thus, we are seeing a bifurcation.

In the future, God's side will be recognized as the supreme good, while Satan's side will be recognized as the supreme evil. Isn't that so? Just because someone is from South Korea, does that mean they are all good people? South Koreans consider other South Koreans to be right. If someone is right-wing, they see what the right does as right. But is that truly right from a higher perspective? If there is any relative relationship with the subject, it will be recognized as overall justice. The details can be adjusted. The question is, where is the center?

Many people have lived throughout history, and many people live on this earth, but the issue is whether they are on God's side or Satan's side. Just because God is not visible does not mean that one does not believe in God; if you do not believe, you will have no way to escape the authority of evil. There is no way to escape the tangled web of Satan that has been woven for 6,000 years. However, if you believe in and rely on God's word, and in the place where life and death are decided, if you can say, "I am on God's side," you will not perish.

So, what must you do to cross over to the realm of good? You must confess, "I was such and such a sinner." You cannot just cross over without doing so. You must settle your accounts and then cross over. That is why the term salvation was established, and the term forgiveness was established. Therefore, the end of days is a time when one can be greatly forgiven, and also a time when one can face great punishment. You must understand this.

On the day of judgment, those who confess before humanity that they were historical sinners can cross over into the realm of historical goodness. Those who can claim to be on God's side in that place can govern both the heavenly world and the earthly world. Only from the position of having settled all that was wandering in the den of sin can one drive out Satan.

That is why the root of sin is the problem. We carry the sins committed by Adam and Eve, as well as the sins of today’s era. That is why we must say, "Heaven! We are a historical race that has betrayed your providence." We must present the condition that we are historical sinners who have betrayed the providential purpose represented by the prophets who have come throughout the ages, from the family of Adam to the family of Noah, the family of Abraham, the family of Moses, Jesus, and if the Lord of the Second Advent comes, to that person as well.

Conditions for Achieving Hope
Everyone, without exception, has hope. To achieve hope, there must be understanding. For understanding to occur, there must be a standard of heart. Is that not so? No one can exclude heart, understanding, and hope. That is why the Bible says that faith, hope, and love must always be present.

So, what is God's hope? God's hope is for us to arrive at the place we truly want to go and live together. Because this world has not become such a place, we are also moving toward that world of hope, the place we truly want to go. God has hope, but there is also a situation. What kind of situation is it? It is a sad situation. If the whole world were filled with joy, it would be a joyful world of hope. However, because we are entangled in a sad situation, even when joyful hope comes, we must pack our bags and leave. That has been the case until now.

No matter how much you pray or how much grace you receive, if the time of hope or the purpose of hope is centered around a world that lives in sin and sad circumstances, it cannot act as eternal. Mornings are different, afternoons are different, and evenings are different. Just as the seasons change, circumstances change in myriad ways, so the grace of heaven cannot maintain a foundation of hope through our lives. The grace received is merely temporary.

Beyond that grace, God gives grace globally. He does not give grace to just one person. He gives it to many saints on earth. Even so, there are more who fall among them. However, even if nine out of ten fall, if one remains, that one becomes the standard to establish ten. If even one person establishes a proper standard, they can elevate it and continue to elevate it. This is how numerous religions and various ethnic forms have emerged.

We have hope. However, because the environment and circumstances do not connect, we seek ways to resolve this. Centered on love or care, ultimately, we aim for ideological unity, starting from life unity to environmental unity. Thus, hope and circumstances must be completely established as the hope of good and the circumstances of good for the garden of good heart to be built. This is the heavenly kingdom on earth that Jesus came to establish and that must be fulfilled upon His return.

So, what is that true place where we will live forever? It is a place where my hope manifests not as relative value but can manifest with my heart and circumstances as universal value. Furthermore, it is a place that can manifest in three-dimensionality. At the same time, in that place, even if one forgets everything, they cannot be unhappy or sad. The more you think about that place, the more joyful it becomes; the more you think about it, the more grateful you feel; the more you think about it, the more joy that cannot be suppressed by your emotions permeates your body. If that happens, everything will be complete.

God's Longed-for Victorious Sons and Daughters
Isn't that right for you too? When your heart is exceedingly joyful, you can forgive all the wrongs of everyone. God also wants to forgive the countless sinners on this earth. Even though they have sinned, He wants to forgive them just as they are. God wants someone to come forth and say, "You have worked hard for humanity with this kind of heart, this kind of hope, and this kind of situation in mind, haven't you?" He desires to comfort us. 

Those who can embrace historical, situational, and future hearts, hopes, and circumstances must appear on this earth in a victorious form and say, "Father! Please release the historical sorrows and grievances up to now." One person must come forth. Why? Because it is necessary to forgive historical sins. If a son can come forth who can relate to God's historical, situational, and future hopes and hearts, God will be very pleased and say, "Oh, my son! What is your wish?" 

What would that son answer? That son would have found it very difficult to cross over from the world of death. It would have been extremely challenging to pave the way through the path of death. However, that son knows well that the struggle to pave this difficult path is the work of the Father, and that humanity's shared fate is to struggle and ultimately build the walls of victory. How could such a son ask, "Take me to heaven and bless me so that I can live indefinitely"? His wish would be to save the sinful humanity of the earth and to subdue the enemy Satan of 6,000 years, saying, "I will do that."

Because we could not call God our Father with our hearts, we could not call God our Father with our circumstances, and we could not call God our Father with our hopes, humanity is struggling today. However, just because one suddenly calls God their Father and says, "Hey, you Satan!" does not mean that Satan will submit. Therefore, the principled standard of sons and daughters that God wanted to establish in heaven must also be established on earth. That principle cannot be ruled by evil. Only then will Satan finally submit.

A historical victor must come forth and return the joy of victory to all people. If such a person appears, humanity can overcome the critical point of judgment. However, Satan will not be forgiven. That time is the time of great judgment. Bringing down fire to destroy the earth is not judgment. How can a God like that be called a God of love? Isn't it the same in the world? When finding a lost child or having a wedding or any joyful event, people forgive past enemies and forget all sad events. God also wants to forgive the countless sinners on earth, but there are no sons and daughters who can stimulate the joy that allows for the forgiveness of humanity.

Look. Even Jesus could not say, "Father, your heart is like this, your situation is like this, and your hope is like this. God! I have fulfilled what you wished, so please rejoice in me." God has forgiven humanity from a place of sorrow until now. He has come out of the realm of sorrow to forgive. Thus, even when forgiven, Satan rushes in again. Until the foundation of sorrow disappears, even after being forgiven, people will continue to sin.

God desires to reach a joyful day when He can say before heaven and earth, "Heaven! Earth! Let my son be exalted. May this joy of today remain forever." He is hoping for a human who can say that.

Look at today's South Korea. When the Second Republic was established, didn't they pardon those who were involved in past incidents under the condition of joy? The same applies to the spiritual world. When thinking about this, you should not be sad that this earth is evil, but rather be sad that you have not found a resolution for yourself. If you cannot resolve it, God will undoubtedly work to establish a being who can fulfill that purpose. Therefore, you must open your eyes wide and earnestly seek such a being.

Do you have the content to call Jesus your friend?
Satan fights day and night to push you into the abyss of eternal death. Satan tirelessly fights to drag you into hell. But what about you? You eat whatever you want and do whatever you wish. Is this acceptable? This cannot continue. Even if your body lives comfortably, your heart must fight day and night.

We call Abraham the father of faith. He was a person who devoted himself to God with all his heart. God demands a heartistic child who connects with Him through such devotion. Therefore, the true child of Abraham is not the child he bore but someone who can call God as Abraham called Him. That person is the true child of Abraham. Similarly, a person who can call God Father as Jesus called Him becomes a brother of Jesus.

A Savior is necessary in a world of sin. After salvation, a Savior is no longer needed. At that point, one becomes a friend. Not only a friend but also a brother. If you can have the disposition to say, "Jesus is my brother," you will not go to hell.

So, do you have the conditions to call Jesus your friend? Do you have the content to be able to call the historical Jesus, the situational Jesus, and the future Jesus your friend?
