At that time, it will be an era where I can directly relate to the Father, where Satan retreats from each of our bodies, and the Father dwells in my heart, allowing us to sing the eternal bond of parent and child, while the entire universe can also offer praise. We know that such a world must come to be, so please help us endure the realistic pain.

We know that there are still bloody hurdles left on the path we must take, and that there are distant and difficult rugged mountains in our way. However, this path is not one we walk alone. The Father has traveled this path tens, hundreds, thousands, and tens of thousands of times before us. 

We also know that it is not the Father who will pave this difficult path, but that humans must pave it themselves. Please allow us to take the final step for the Father who has worked hard to come this far. The path remains, so even if we fall along the way, let us step on the footprints the Father walked and follow the bloodstains the Father left behind.

When we offer this torn and wounded body as a living sacrifice before the Father, we know that the Father will establish the position of the child before all the world and bless us. We understand that we must reach such a place, so please do not let us tire until we get there.

Every time we grow weary, the Father has supported us, and every time we feel despair and loneliness, heaven has urged us. Please do not let us forget that before we labor, the Father has worked for us hundreds, thousands of times.

We have learned how difficult it is to connect with human beings who have substance as an incorporeal being and to stimulate and awaken them. It has been the Father who has tirelessly paved this path. Because there is Satan who opposes without rest, the Father has continuously worked hard to pave this path, fighting tirelessly for the sake of my individual life. Please fill our hearts with a deep yearning to hold onto the Father with a humble heart. Let the sorrowful heart that calls out to the Father explode in each of our hearts.

We know that the Father comforts such people and gathers them, promising a new world of covenant and a divine achievement. Therefore, until that position is confirmed, please allow us to endure to the end and become sons and daughters who can raise the glory of victory and the fruits of victory before all creation.

15)
Living with Conviction
<Summary of the Message> Let us become people who live with conviction. The fate of every human being is determined by their attitude (conviction and direction) between the ages of 18 and 24. The results of living with conviction only appear after a long time. A person without conviction, no matter how splendid their reality may be, is likely to break along the way, while a person with conviction may face minor difficulties but can endure until the end.

Even a knowledgeable person cannot stand against a person with conviction. That is why the scriptures say to give your heart, mind, and character, but not to give your knowledge. A person with conviction does not break even when faced with many twists and turns; they overcome and move forward. Thus, the results are even more brilliant.

There is not only human conviction but also universal conviction, and furthermore, there is God's conviction. God's history has been to guide history with the goal of uniting God's conviction with human conviction, and religion has emerged as a means of achieving this. God's conviction is the conviction to achieve the purpose of creation. Its content is to love heaven first, love humanity, and love the entire universe. In other words, God's purpose of creation is to establish a world centered on love among heaven, earth, and humanity.

In the end, those who possess such conviction will never be judged nor perish.

16)
The Lord of the Second Advent and the Third Israel
<Summary of the Message> All creation groans because of our human fall, and therefore, we must restore this. Since humanity was created after all things, we must undergo a separation to restore all things. We are fighting not only against ourselves but also against Satan. When we lack the intelligence to judge this will, we must obey unconditionally.

To make atonement, we take things as conditions. The reason we offer our tithes before heaven is also here. The number 9 represents the needs of the fallen world, while the number 10 represents the number that transcends this, the number of the heavenly world.

The seeds of all creation were first taken by fallen humanity. Therefore, this must be sanctified. In the return of the Israelite nation to Canaan, there was also a three-year period of sanctification. Every seed of every plant must be left as sanctified. We must green this peninsula with our own hands. Seeing many mountains turn green with trees, this greening is easy. We must plant trees for 120 to 360 weeks throughout our lives. Humanity must leave an eternal connection to the earth. We must do this for the next three years.

Jesus also sought to make atonement for 4,000 years of history in 2 years and 8 months. The reason Jesus had three disciples was to establish beloved sons and daughters. Thus, Jesus aimed to become the ancestor of the first Israel and to establish the second Israel. To become the ancestor of the first Israel, he had to gather the 12 tribes at that time. Therefore, he appointed three disciples and twelve disciples as representatives of the first Israel. However, because they could not unite with Jesus, Israel was destroyed. Thus, the will he sought to accomplish has extended to find the first and second Israel.

The Christians who died after Jesus formed the first Israel in the spirit world. This could not be accomplished on earth and was instead realized in the spiritual world. Earthly Christian believers correspond to the first Israel during Jesus' time.

The Lord of the Second Advent must come as the ancestor of not only the third Israel but also the first and second Israel. Our family must stand in a position like the children in the Father's womb, transcending the doubts of the first Israel during Jesus' time, through the heart of the Father. The Lord of the Second Advent must govern the spirit world. By governing the spirit world, he must start from the foundation of establishing the first Israel. Those in the spirit world do not have a connection with the True Parents, so they must go through this process. There is a type of the twelve tribes in the spirit world, but the Christianity that must become the second Israel has lost the center to form tribes. Therefore, we must establish a unified ideology to organize the tribes.

We must realize the purpose of returning to Canaan that the Israelite people born in Egypt could not achieve during their 40 years in the wilderness, just as Joshua and Caleb accomplished it with firm faith and courage. And we must organize the tribes. Therefore, we must establish Christianity as a tribe of the second Israel. To achieve this, we must go through a path of adversity reminiscent of Jesus' three years of public ministry.

We must send the first Israel to the spirit world and establish the second Israel on earth, using it as a foundation to establish the third Israel on earth. The history of Christianity over the past 2,000 years has been to find and establish the second Israel that Jesus could not find. Since Christianity has not fulfilled its responsibility to establish the second Israel, we must become the ancestors of the second Israel. We must find and establish a second Israel that can freely relate to Jesus. Now, for the next three years, this is a period for fundamental restoration to establish this. We must find our children with the heart of a parent. To become parents, we must give birth to children. We must become like the children born through the womb of the Father and the womb of the Mother. To do this, we must establish children of Cain-like faith and place them in a position similar to Abel-like kin, thus standing in the position of restoring Cain and Abel.

The Lord of the Second Advent must pass through the hearts of the first, second, and third Israel.

Until now, it has been a time to find just Adam, so the mother and son have cooperated, but from now on, the father and daughter must cooperate.

We must be granted the authority to bless our children of faith. We must become dutiful children who can hold onto and comfort the hearts of parents who have fallen while searching for their sons.

Our standard of character is determined by how much the Father will shed tears when we weep. The Father, who has sought for 6,000 years, must also be able to weep, losing his dignity. Even fallen parents in the world feel that when their beloved children are dying, they would have the heart to save them, even if heaven and earth were to collapse. How much more so would the God of love?

It is okay to forget everything. However, we must be able to shed tears that can move heaven, touch our brothers, and stir the earth. Evangelism must be done with the heart of finding lost children in place of the Father. Even if we must endure prison, we must do this. We must penetrate hell to find heaven. Thus, we must restore from the lowest to the highest.

Even if the teacher goes, the will will surely be fulfilled. Therefore, we intend to fight a good and wise fight. We can only advance to the position of parents after first creating adopted children.

Let us become those who do not leave behind any regrets after hearing these words. I hope that for just three years, you will remain steadfast in your determination.

<Prayer> Father, now we bow before your knees, so please give us your instructions one by one.

We are like little children. Moreover, we are like naked and hungry children. We have wounds on our bodies and are starving. Do not forsake your sons and daughters gathered here. When you are sad, may we also be sad; when you are joyful, may we also be joyful; when you feel wronged, may we also feel wronged, so that we can speak through our hearts, receive through our hearts, and become one through our hearts.

If this is not possible, we know that we cannot melt the hearts of the thirty million people living in this land, which is like a wasteland, a wilderness, and a desolate empty field. The path that God's people must walk

That is how it will be fair. We must stand in opposition to any ideology that takes life with sovereignty. Such a time must come. It is an inevitable historical path that must be traversed. Otherwise, the way will be blocked.

Humanity is in a historical destiny to fight and seek for that time, emulating the will of God, the subject of the heart. There can be no path of struggle in humanity emulating God and moving toward God's goal, and history records these twists and turns.

It has been a historical path of such struggles. The ultimate remains of the Lord  
Because history has started with such twists and turns, we have walked in undesired directions, and Heaven has also pioneered undesired paths from a position more difficult than our humanity. No. In the end, what ideology must it be? It must be heartism. That will, that ideology is Godism. This Godism can be my ideology, and God's will can be my will, and when that ideology and I are emotionally connected, and when that connection cannot be severed for any worldly wealth and glory, then the final destination will arrive.  
As we face such a time in the end, we must broaden our perspective and critically evaluate the world. We cannot rely on the historical view we have learned so far. The direction is different. History may seem to flow aimlessly, but there is a motive behind its flow. It is not within itself, but it is being turned from above or from afar.  
Why is that? If there is a sovereign in any country, does that sovereign want to perish? No sovereign of any nation wants to perish. Every sovereign wants to dominate the world and put all people under their control. However, things do not go as desired. Isn’t that so? Those sovereigns desire such nations and states, but why do the crises of death come, and why do the crises of ruin come? We must understand that the miserable reality of the historical path is that things happen that were not wished for. Therefore, this itself must not become the motive and the solution. The motive and solution lie elsewhere.  
That is why humanity is wandering in search of the world of motives and the world of results. Then, what should that motive and result be? It must not be a motive arising from humanity, but a motive arising from God, and it must not be a result arising from humanity, but a result arising from God. If it is true, it must start and end with God. If that happens, the problem is simple, and we have become the ones who endure. Humanity has become the motive and humanity has become the result, so these motives and results are inextricably tangled. Therefore, without removing the motives and results of humanity, we cannot transfer new motives and results. To transfer this, God has worked infinitely hard.  
God, if there is a path of death in today’s human world, must have stood in a position above that, and if there is a path of suffering, He must have walked a path of suffering that is even more severe. Isn’t that so? To prevent humanity from falling into the abyss of death requires several times the strength. Isn’t that right? Can it be done with the strength that rolls in? It requires several times that strength. If there is a will of Heaven to save this earth, it must dissect and excise the corrupt and decayed places. For this, we must understand that there are beings other than humans who are enduring several tens or hundreds of times the suffering that I am experiencing today. The purpose of religion is to make this known. If God is carrying out the providence of salvation, where is the reason? It is to make these facts known and to align the heart of God with the heart of humanity in one direction.  
The individual as the reflection of heaven and earth  
As I mentioned to you at the beginning, the sorrow and suffering of this society and era are connected to me and reflected in me; unless we fill the abyss of sorrow and suffering that seeps into your heart and body, there is no way to remove the misfortunes and twists of this world related to you. That is why Jesus did not say that there is a relative place of heaven on this earth. He said that heaven is in your heart. Unless heaven is established in the heart, heaven cannot be established in any other place. Therefore, we must not be discouraged, no matter how evil this world is. We must recognize that this world is a world connected to me and reflected in me, and we must discover what is incomplete in ourselves and become those who complete it. If there is something to lament and curse, one must become someone who can curse oneself, and from that position, the path to revival will be opened.  
The world and humanity are formed by individuals gathering together. Therefore, in the end times, all of humanity in the world is like one person. The events occurring throughout the world are akin to those happening on the stage of one person's life. It can be seen as a reflection of one person's heart and body. Then, how can we achieve victory in the end? We must gather our hearts and become one with our bodies to achieve victory. Similarly, something must emerge that can gather the hearts of humanity across the globe and unify them with the bodily stage of human life.  
The individual is a microcosm of the universe, a reflection of heaven and earth, and a being that represents heaven and earth. Therefore, I can be the master of my family, the master of society, the master of the nation, the master of the world, and the master of heaven and earth.  
We must become such individuals. When the heart and body, which represent heaven and earth and are reflections of heaven and earth, completely align with the world of the heart and body of reality—completely in harmony, completely automatic, completely independent—then the entire universe will be influenced by that person. The principle is established that way.  
However, humanity lost such an individual due to the fall, so we must recover that individual. We must seek it. The one who comes with such a character is the Lord. The coming Lord is the one who can move heaven with the heart and move the earth with the body.  
The path the Lord must endure  
So how must one become such a central being? Looking at Jacob as a central figure, he had to go through a path of suffering, sacrifice, and the willingness to face death to become the central being recognized by heaven in his family. He had to overcome all difficulties of the familial environment.

The Savior needed in this land.

If you build for your family, the nation will be destroyed. If you build for your nation, the world will be destroyed, and if you build for the world, God will destroy it. Then what is the most central thing that cannot be wrong? It is serving God.  
Filial sons and daughters who resolve God's resentment.  
As we go through the historical path of God's restoration providence, our ancestors have shed blood and crossed the peaks of death. Even in the world, when someone suffers unjustly, there is support and cooperation. Those who suffer unjustly have allies. Our Korean nation also has many allies because it has suffered unjustly. No matter how difficult the situation, we will not starve to death anymore.  
So what must this nation do now? We must hold onto God. We must hold onto God. God has never appealed to anyone when He is unjustly treated and indignant. He has never appealed to humans. Even when conscientious people go to the point of death unjustly, they do not wish for this country to recognize them. They only wished for God to recognize them. If individuals are like that, then families must be like that, and nations must be like that as well. Therefore, the thirty million people of this unjust nation must unite their hearts and launch a movement saying, “God, please recognize us.” Then we will not perish.  
Let’s think again. When we say, “God, please recognize us,” we must consider what God's position will be. It is not only us who are unjustly treated and indignant. God is in a position of greater injustice, greater indignation, and greater pity than we are. Why? When God sees His beloved sons and daughters, the good side being treated unjustly and suffering, does He say, “Oh, well done”? No, He feels the pain of His heart breaking and melting. God experiences a sorrow greater than the sorrow we endure as He looks upon us.  
When this nation knows only the heart of God, it will dominate heaven and earth. Why is that? Even if there are many children and many people, the greatest loyal subject, filial child, and virtuous woman is one person. Even if the parents of fallen humans have the same children, it is natural to think more of the child who is being treated unjustly; how much more so for God?  
Therefore, at this time, we must not appeal to God about the suffering of our nation, but rather we must say, “How does the Father feel as He looks upon this nation? Please do not suffer because of our suffering. We will willingly walk the path of suffering. Do not suffer because of the path of death. We will walk that path.” We must have that firm resolution. Only then can we become the greatest loyal subjects recognized by heaven and earth at the critical moment of determining the final loyal subject.  
What is God looking for? God is not looking for a certain people but is looking for the most beloved loyal sons and daughters. He wants to find and establish loyal sons and daughters to boast to that people. He seeks to gather the world, find one nation, establish Israel, gather one bloodline, find one family, and gather one family to find one person. Finding that one person is finding the world, so that one person must possess a heart that can resolve all of God's historical grievances. Only when such a loyal son appears can the wicked receive atonement through him.  
We have learned that when we are in a position of injustice, heaven feels even greater injustice. To transition into a new era, one must go through the processes of historical connections, providential connections, and emotional connections. In going through such a path, we must not just look on as our nation suffers unjustly. The heart of the Father who sees this is in greater pain, so we must stand in that place with a joyful heart. We must say, “Please forgive us and forgive the world as you look upon us.” If we can become such people, we will undoubtedly become the beloved sons and daughters of God, inherit the legacy of heaven and earth, and all nations will bow before us. I am confident of this. History flows in that way.  
The workers of the new era.  
I have delivered this message to you gathered here today. Let us move forward. In this nation of many sorrows, let us not say that the cause of this nation's grief lies with any sovereign. Let us say, “It is my responsibility, our responsibility. They are our representatives.” When they are sorrowful, we must also be sorrowful, and when they suffer, we must also suffer. This is the path we must take.  
Looking at the fate of this nation, the only direction we can go is this path.  
This is my work; if there is sorrow in the nation, I can say that it is my sorrow, and all people! Do not appeal your sorrow to God but to us. I hope to become a son or daughter who can say that. Do you understand?  
Even if we have sorrow, we must not let it end with our sorrow. We must stand before the nation and say, “Bring all your sorrows to us,” and if there is a group that rises up to take responsibility for their sorrows with death, sacrifice, and patience, that group will become the substantial beings representing God's will and will be the masters who can judge good and evil on this earth. For 6,000 years, God has been waiting to see from which nation or denomination such groups will emerge. They have suffered greater pain than us, crossed greater peaks of death than us, and have sought a resting place with hearts filled with more sorrow than ours, struggling to find it. We must acknowledge this aspect of the Father.  
Knowing this aspect of the Father, we must realize that the labor He has done in the historical path is for me, that the labor He has done for the providential will of this era is for me, and that the labor He will do for the hope of the future is also for me. We must recognize that we have the connection to become filial children before the Father who has labored for us. Only those who can step forward and say that they will take responsibility on behalf of all people will become the workers of the new era and will be the ones entrusted with the work of heaven in the new era.  
That is why the Lord who is to come at the end will not come riding on clouds. He must not come riding on clouds. He is the Prince of Suffering, the Prince of Persecution, and the Prince of Patience. Even while receiving the greatest persecution and harboring the deepest resentment and sorrow, He embraces the world, saying, “Father, this is what I must rightfully endure as a human being, so please do not feel hurt or sorrow for me. Please do not think of it with a heavy heart. This is now my responsibility.”  
He must be one who takes upon Himself all the pain and death of humanity and fulfills the Father's responsibility on this earth to become the Savior. God has suffered to establish such a personality.  
This is the title I mentioned to you earlier.  
What has heaven endured for us? We must understand the inner pain of God who has suffered for us. People live a short life of 70 or 80 years, saying they have many enemies and that their environment is not comfortable. If an individual, who is a reflection of heaven and earth, is like that, how must God, who is the subject of that individual and the subject of the earth, have felt? For 6,000 years, there has not been a single day when God's tears have dried.  
You may wonder what kind of tears God sheds. Where did your tears begin? God also has emotions. If humans, created by God, have emotions, then it goes without saying that God has them too.  
Satan is the great enemy for 6,000 years.  
Although humanity on this earth is the offspring of the fall, God Himself, being of His own bloodline and direct children, comes with the heart of a parent seeking lost sons and daughters, with feelings beyond that. Therefore, the scenes where we shed tears over this land, where we collapse in death and pain, and where we are overwhelmed with sorrow reflect God's sorrow and grief. Thus, individuals, families, and nations that despise good people, persecute good people, and kill good people will not last long. Why? Because God remembers that.  
Therefore, we must recognize that every time our tears fall, heaven's tears fall as well. Whenever we feel indignation and deep pain toward our enemies, we must understand that God sheds tears of forgiveness. God is not the one who says, “Ah, you deserved to die.” He does not regard people as enemies.
is not. If there is a great enemy from 6,000 years ago, it is not a person but Satan who lures people. Satan is the enemy. 
If a great judge were to pass the highest sentence on a prisoner, he should be able to shed tears for them. The individual human is extremely good. That being with features is the holy body that represents the entire universe. Because the evil that moves the heart of such a body is bad, the authority to judge that evil exists, but there is no authority to judge that body. A judge who can shed tears will not be caught in heaven. If you go before heaven with a heart that is not like this, with an illegal and unjust heart, what will happen? 
Heaven strikes down nations that curse other nations. It mocks those who laugh at nations that are judged and fall. Our Korean people have been trampled upon by many nations throughout history, but this nation holds no grudges against others. It is a nation that does not know invasion. From what I see, this is a grateful thing. This nation knows how to shed tears and lament in the right place, but it does not know how to blame others. When I see this, I feel that there is hope for this nation. 
Dear friends, is there a person in front of you who is a sworn enemy? That person is not the enemy. The traitor who confronts the nation and ideology is not human but the great enemy Satan. 
God who bears the burdens of humanity alone 
Do you know how much God desired for heaven and earth to become one? From the moment our ancestors were expelled from the Garden of Eden, God has longed for humanity to become one with Him through the heart of a father and son. If humanity had not fallen and had not betrayed heaven, enemies would not have arisen, and we would have already welcomed an ideal world. The scientific civilization of today, like the 20th century, would have been achieved thousands of years ago. Modern civilization has been built over the 400 years since the Renaissance. Today, we boast that we have constructed this civilization over 400 years, but if God had intervened directly, this world of civilization might have been built in 40 years, or even in one generation. 
However, since complications arose, God has come forth to bear the history of suffering to establish one ideology and bring unity. Throughout His dealings with nations and states, there is not a single place in this universe where He has not left His footprints. Every time a good person falls, there are God's tears shed there. A good lineage does not perish. Where God's sons and daughters are persecuted and oppressed, there fall God's droplets of sweat. No one can occupy those tears and sweat of God. Not even Satan. 
Evil is essentially about using others, while good is about being used. The essence of Satan, which has the nature of using, cannot dominate the essence of being used. To dominate, it must also become like that. Therefore, the path of virtue is inherently about serving. The tears shed by those who have fallen to elevate the essence of serving are God's tears, and their blood and sweat are God's blood and sweat. 
This nation is currently in a state of confusion. Young men and women, we have blood and flesh. In our hearts, emotions flow. Every time the heart beats, blood surges through the arteries and veins. There is sweat and tears flowing through bones, flesh, and blood. For whom do we shed this? It is good to fall for the nation. It is good to fall for any ideology. But above all, we must fall for God. Then you will not perish. 
Look at the nation of Israel. After Jesus came and went, they became a nation that has been persecuted for 2,000 years. No matter what society they enter, they have been oppressed by that society, yet today, they control the world's economy, and the new culture has emerged from their foundation. When they were whipped, they gritted their teeth and called out to God with tears. As long as this historical process remains, God could not help but be sad. 
The path and responsibility of the unification warriors 
Today, you are kneeling in this Unification Church. The people of this Unification Church are being oppressed. The person speaking here also has grievances and feelings of injustice. I have no enemies. If my existence can be pushed aside for the blessing of this nation, I am someone who wishes for that. 
Unification family members, blood flows in our hearts. However, the day the blood flowing through our limbs stops is the day we die. Do not forget that you have a father, and until the moment of death, sweat for this purpose. If you struggle with a firm resolve to achieve this purpose without extending it to future generations, you will not perish. 
When a beloved child is beaten, how desperately must God have wanted to trample down the nation that is striking? However, the goal is to destroy the enemy, not to destroy people, so He could not do so. God hates the enemy but loves people. 
We must understand that if we blame and curse heaven and earth, heaven will be sad and Satan will rejoice. Therefore, even if we say we have repaid the enemy, we must shed tears for humanity. That is how it should be. 
Unification warriors, there are many paths of struggle ahead of us. There are still thorny paths left. This does not end with solving any problems of this nation, but there is a path that must go beyond the world to the heavenly realm. The tears you shed on this path are the tears that are motivated by the deepest feelings of the Father from 6,000 years ago and the tears shed for the world where God can dance in joy for millions of years. As you move toward that world, you must charge forward vigorously without knowing how to fall. 
Then, from here, the circumstances that God has suffered will be resolved. In this way, God will say, "Oh, beloved sons and daughters, there were many people living on earth, but there was no one who fought on behalf of my heart, and now you stand in the same position as me and fight." 
This is the appearance of the Unification group that is being oppressed. We who must walk the narrow path must overcome the circumstances of lamentation and declare that we will bear the grievances of this nation upon ourselves and take responsibility for the global oppression. 
Father, I will take responsibility for all of this, so let what I suffer today be accepted as the suffering of future generations, and let me be able to say, "I am suffering for the world." 
Then we will not perish. 
The teacher has asked you to shed tears from now on as you go forward. He has asked you to shed blood and sweat. Those standing here have fought like that. They are not those who make excuses and try to escape. If you shed tears, I do not mind shedding blood; if you shed sweat, I do not mind shedding tears. Without this, we cannot turn the path of the nation. 
Today, you must not end with merely hearing this teacher's advice in words. We must understand the historical struggles that heaven has endured for us. No matter what we have suffered, we cannot compare it to the struggles that heaven has faced, and no matter how unjust we feel, we cannot compare it to God's feelings of injustice. 
We are a lineage of historical sin. I sincerely hope that all of you who are present here today do not leave as mere visitors. 
We are humanity that harbors feelings of injustice and resentment. Therefore, we must not only cut out that grievance but also welcome God and take responsibility for the fight against Satan, and furthermore, we must be in a position to embrace and love the poor. God has raised us to fulfill His work, so I ask that you become those who can take on this responsibility. 
<Prayer> Father, as I deliver this message, I feel extremely inadequate. How much did you want to cry out, how much did you want to weep, how much did you want to stomp your feet? I understand the circumstances of the Father who, due to His heavenly dignity and reputation, has a heart that longs to cry but cannot. 
Father, may we, who have come through the historical course, turn our reflections toward the world and bear the world's reflections within ourselves, becoming filial sons and daughters who can welcome the Father who moves this world. I know this is the Father's wish, and I also understand that we must not let the enemy stand before the Father but take responsibility ourselves. I earnestly hope and desire that from now on, we can be sons and daughters who can stand boldly before heaven with a new determination to sacrifice for this purpose. 
Even if a rough path comes before us and persecution may arise, let us think of the Father; even if tears rise in loneliness, let us think of the Father; even when we are overwhelmed by the sorrows of life and do not know where to turn, let us think of the Father and consider this path as the path we must walk, the path we must take in our lives, and if we can do so with gratitude, we know we will not perish. Through such people, this nation will come to know a new direction, and the time will come when a new cultural standard and perspective for all humanity will be established. Therefore, let us surpass the standards of human affection and establish the ties of heavenly destiny, becoming warriors who raise our arms high and march to build the garden of heavenly heart. Let us be your sons and daughters who march toward the enemy's front lines to see the end of Satan. Thus, may we be sons and daughters who can find the lost humanity and return them to the embrace of heaven, singing the song of victory. I earnestly hope and desire this, Father. 
At this time, to the sons and daughters who are following the lonely ones in various places in South Korea, shedding tears with lonely hearts, may you allow them to know this moment through the ties of your heart and inherit the heart of heaven to fulfill their responsibilities. May they be sons and daughters who can embrace the poor as their own children, take responsibility, and fight against Satan, and moreover, may they be sons and daughters who can serve and show filial piety to the Father. 
May you embrace us so that we are not lacking in taking on the historical mission, the global mission, and furthermore, the cosmic mission that heaven wishes to entrust to us, and I earnestly ask and desire this, offering all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. 
Focus on the night worship 
<Summary of the message> Focus on the night worship. Think of the evangelists who have gone out to the regions. Be sure to bring them back with successful evangelism. 
Faith issues are issues of eternal life. 
When you go to bed at night, do you have the shoes you took off the night before? 
No matter how busy you are, there is nothing more important than the issue of eternal life in this world. 
The reason people fall away is that they do not have a serious feeling that the issue of eternal life is being determined in this world. 
The teacher also never thinks about death. 
When you go to heaven and many nations welcome you, if you have not formed a heart connection with those nations, you will have no face to meet them. 
What the teacher knows is not at the level that you know. 
When you are in a position to have children, you want to have good children. The teacher feels the same. He does not want to have disabled children. He does not want to have beggar-like children. 
Do not ridicule the beggars or the disabled in the streets. Think that your spiritual body may look like that. 
You must become someone who can share what you have with others. 
Do not think you are still young. Everyone has lived like that and passed away. 
Put in all your sincerity. Live the best life possible. Do not loosen your tension for even a minute or a second. 
Strive to gather. Move. 
How capable is Satan? You are destined to confront Satan who has been trained for 6,000 years. 
Can you play around and confront Satan? You must make an effort, even if it means hitting. It is not for the teacher. The teacher can go to a place where he can die now. Even if it is not you, the purpose can still be fulfilled. However, the reason for the suffering and hardship is to stand before heaven. 
Bring evangelism to the night worship. Otherwise, the prestige of the headquarters will not stand. Whether you are a student or an adult, even those at the headquarters must go out and evangelize. Whatever the situation at home or your own circumstances, that is a personal matter, not heaven's matter. You must have a heart that cannot show your face. 
The names of the leaders and class leaders are nice, but they are not just names. Take responsibility. 
Restoration is fundamental restoration. 
<Picture: 010250.jpg> 
Whether male or female, you must become an existence that has not yet been born, like a being in the mother's womb. 
You should rejoice together when there is joy, and be sad together when there is sadness. 
I have no desire to stay at the headquarters. 
I have no desire to preach. 
The responsibilities of the teacher have been fulfilled. Now only each person's responsibility remains. 
No one is in a daze. I am stating the facts. 
You will know when you die, even if you do not know now. 
You must be there before the teacher during worship. 
No matter what path you take, you must go ahead of the teacher. 
From now on, it is time to go out and make your own children of faith. 
While others go out to evangelize, are you just sleeping at home? Those over 40 must be busier. There is no time. 
Moreover, wives and women must work even harder. Women have many sins. 
Starting next week, I plan to go out to the regions instead of staying at the headquarters. 
I must take on collective responsibility and move. 
Will you just watch someone fall into a pit? You must go after them and save them, even if it means breaking their legs. The teacher does not work with you in a leisurely manner. He works with his life on the line. 
Even if you are resting, the teacher keeps going. Now he is going down. He is going back. When it gets a little dark, when he loses strength, he must go, but he cannot. That is it. 
Newcomers are fast. 
You cannot always give for your own sake. You are working for the Father and all humanity. The destination is not here. Even now, you are still on the way. 
Even if it means saying harsh words, you must make sure that work is done. 
You are still in a state of development, as if you have not even put on your shoes. 
This time is both the last and the first. Getting a job is not the issue. You must go out to evangelize. If there are circumstances, you must evangelize at your workplace. 
Do not say you know the teacher. The teacher only knows the principles. He only knows the principles and rules. You know through that. 
Evangelize. Make children of faith through evangelism. At least three must be made. Put in your utmost sincerity. 
You cannot do it with leftovers. 
Heaven took 6,000 years to find one son. You are within the benefits that can establish all in just six months. 
Now, you must become one with the teacher emotionally. You must become one with the heart of the parents. 
It is the time of birth. 
Moreover, how precious is it to evangelize this year? Let us evangelize before this year ends. Originally, next year, the second generation should go out, and the year after that, the third generation should go out to evangelize. 
The teacher only knows the principles. He only knows those who are based on principles and rules. 
Have you ever stayed up all night to evangelize? The teacher has stayed up many nights. They will ask you in the spirit world how many nights you have stayed up to evangelize. Moreover,
This three-year period is a time to devote all one's strength to evangelism. *

If you do not give and receive, you will die.
<Summary of the Word> The rear must support the front materially, in action, and emotionally. If you do not give and receive, you will die. The ideal world is one where the whole serves the individual, and the individual serves the whole. Originally, one must relate to three above and three below centered on oneself. Thus, one must achieve the number seven. *
October 21, 1960 (Friday) night after the joint meeting, at the former headquarters church.

18)
Live with history.
<Summary of the Word> There must be homes and villages, towns, counties, provinces, and nations where the Father can rest and pass through. Even if you prepare a room, you must prepare a heavenly room and a public room. Even if you cook rice, you must cook heavenly rice and public rice. When precious guests come from outside, there must be at least three places in a village to show them around and host them. In the future, there must be competition to build churches better among each other. The world will become a place where the competition is about who is more loyal to others. Thus, the most loyal person will become the representative and succeed. The teacher thinks not of life issues but of eternal life issues. In the future, we will set the standard for eternal families and eternal individuals. Even when we wear clothes or eat food, if we live thinking of those who are not as fortunate, we will be blessed. The line is not formed around one person. It is determined by moving for others rather than oneself and for the future rather than the present. If you work for society, you will be remembered within the social realm; if you work for the nation, you will be remembered within the national realm; if you work for the world, you will be remembered within the world realm. You will be remembered to the extent that you have worked for others. Also, the longer you work for others, the more you will be remembered. 
October 23, 1960 (Sunday), Asan, Chungcheongnam-do. 
* This word is organized from notes provided by Chairman Yoo Gwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee of the Association, with the title added by the editor. 

19)
Good people.
<Summary of the Word> Everyone wants to be a good person and do good deeds. So, what kind of person is the best person in the world? To someone who does not know, it would be a teacher. To an orphan, it would be someone who raises them. In the nation, it would be a leader who helps the citizens live happily. Among them, the best person would be someone who moves the earthly and spiritual beings from the place of death to the place of life. What kind of person saves me? It is someone who has what others do not have. He is someone who possesses God. Therefore, the best person is one who regards God as their Father and lives with God within their sphere of life. *
October 23, 1960 (Sunday), Asan, Chungcheongnam-do. 
* This word is organized from notes provided by Chairman Yoo Gwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee of the Association, with the title added by the editor. 

20)
Living a life that distinguishes good and evil.
<Summary of the Word> Without the desire to distinguish between good and evil, one cannot live a life of good. Each aspect of my life must be examined to determine whether it starts from a motive of good and is moving toward good. The motive of good is not the self but God. Without the consciousness of good, there is no public outrage against evil. *
October 30, 1960 (Sunday), Suduksa, Yesan, Chungnam. 
* This word was spoken at a gathering of members from three churches in Hongseong, Haemi, and Galsan in Chungnam, organized from notes recorded by Chairman Yoo Gwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee of the Association. 

21)
The one and only Father.
<Summary of the Word> In the future, one should not look to the headquarters or district for support. Just as one cannot receive support when giving birth to their own children, one must take responsibility for their own home. Heaven does not desire an easily established foundation. It desires a foundation built with blood, sweat, and tears. Do not owe your brothers but make your brothers owe you. Humanity on this earth is born with the blood of the fall, regardless of right or wrong. We are a fallen race. How much disgust have we felt toward the fallen self! Feeling this is the first external step to returning to the unfallen self. If we leave this pitiful humanity as it is, it will perish. There is one who has raised, awakened, and saved this humanity; that person is none other than the embodiment of goodness and love. He is the one and only Father. He has paved the way while you were unaware and has come to find you. He is the one who completes all things. He is the one who cannot be exchanged for anything, even if the entire universe is given. He is the protagonist who shed blood when we did not think of him, who shed tears, and who sweated. To dedicate everything for him is religion. There are many religions, but that one and only Father has never been able to plead with any religion. Because there is an enemy, the Father must find someone to ask for repayment. If that one person, that one filial child had come to this earth, history would not have turned out this way. If there is a king of service in a society that knows only itself, there will be mutual opposition. Goodness is not for oneself but for others. The suffering we endure is to resemble the Father. We must become the Father’s clothes, shoes, or the ground he walks on. The Father is the protagonist of the universe and is not bound by anything. He is the center of all the highest values we think of. The Father, who sheds sweat, tears, and blood for us, must be repented to. We must repent for not even knowing the Father’s name. We must call out to that Father, who we cannot call enough, with the deep heart of six thousand years. No matter how difficult it is, you must be moved to be able to call him Father. The teacher shed many tears when you shed tears, and he prayed much when you peacefully slept. Even if many people live here, if there are only three sons who can hold hands and say, "What is yours is mine, and what is mine is yours," this land will not perish. If there are a few hundred such people among thirty million, this nation will not perish. That kind of emotion must burn to solve the problem. Do not say that you do not have gold and silver treasures. 
You are my Father, and I am your son, so please tell me the situations you have not yet addressed and the concerns you wish to express. You must become children who can do. The Father had no sons, daughters, nations, or people. He had the heartfelt desire to call someone his son but could not do so. 
Call the one and only Father as a true Father. The purpose of walking this path is to truly call the Father, Father. The Father does not come to find a capable person or a capable nation. He comes to find sons and daughters who are willing to do heavenly work, even if it is difficult. The Korean people are pitiful. They stand in a position where they must resolve whether to live or die. 
Purifying body and mind, shedding all faults, and meeting the Father in a naked state is the principle of baptism. Therefore, the way is to abandon everything. It may be unfair if the ugly person gathers, but we are not ugly. It was good to be pitiful. The teacher boasts of having no money before his family. 
We must go for six hundred million or seven hundred million years. The teacher is compassionate but also merciless. Just thinking of that one Father makes one weep. If he is wronged, he is the most wronged, and if he is angry, he is the most angry. We have come to embrace him as our Father and to raise the banner of unification. We must advance to the position of judging the enemy with the spirit of this unification. 
Today, there are 2.7 to 8 billion people, and the Father will not turn back until the end. He will not return without making Satan surrender. The teacher has come for history, the world, and countless people. He has come hoping for a new heaven and earth for all humanity. He has come not to escape hell but to return to the very bottom. 
If not eating is suffering, then starve. If not wearing is suffering, then strip. If sweating is hard, then sweat. There must be one more thing that is better than the satanic world. 
What is unification? It is to become one with the Father. To unify, first, we must unify our lives. There is no stage of life for the Father on earth. Therefore, we must unify centered on the Father’s way of life. Second, we must unify our actions. We must unify our actions centered on the Father’s heart. Even if our lives are different, even if our actions are different, the life and action centered on that heart must be the same. Third, we must unify our ideologies. 
Satan is the enemy of God. The enemy of God is my enemy. We must take responsibility and go forward. Satan strikes and steals, and then perishes. But heaven takes after being struck and comes out. 
Three years is enough. I believe that completing the first stage of the mission can be done in three years. Even at the table where you eat, do it with the Father. Even in the place where you sleep, do it with the Father. Do everything in that whole place with the Father. Do not be conscious of your brothers but do it with the Father. 
Father, what are you doing? I will do it with you. Father, where are you going? I will go with you. Father, whom do you love? I will love with you. You must establish an inseparable bond with the Father. Then you will not regret attending this gathering today and will remember it forever. *
22)
The mission of the earthly saints.
<Summary of the Word> Each of you is a person who has come out alive from the 6,000 years of providential history, so you must indemnify the position of Adam, the position of Jesus, and the position of the Lord of the Second Advent to be complete. 
We must now indemnify the position of Jesus, who is the first fruit, and since we are the next fruit, we must resolve the position of Jesus. Therefore, we must give birth to children of faith. 
We, who must do greater works than Jesus, must give birth to Abel-like children and establish Cain-like children of faith. Only then will the children of the Jesus type and the Lord of the Second Advent type be united. 
We must offer more than three times the sincerity that has brought the Holy Spirit. While the teacher has the spirit world as a fence, the mother must have the earth as a fence. Therefore, now is the time of women and the time of cows. 
Just as a baby is born after passing through the mother’s womb, all of humanity must take the position of having passed through the mother’s womb to be reborn. 
Many good spirits have sacrificed to find one Adam. Therefore, there will also be sacrifices in the process of finding the mother. 
We want to forget the wrongs before serving the mother. However, we cannot forgive those who accuse us because of the mother. If they accuse us of doing something because the mother did it, that will be a big problem. 
November 3, 1960 (Thursday), from 10 PM to 1:30 AM the next day, at the former headquarters church ondol room.

Our determination.
Matthew 10:32-42
<Prayer (I)> Father! We have come to understand the sorrow you have endured to find your original sons and daughters lost for 6,000 years. We also understand that you have never been able to hold and share your circumstances with a single human being whom you could bless as your sons and daughters. 
Among many nations, you love this pitiful nation, and especially love this land and this country, Father! Although this nation is poor and insignificant, we know that there are hidden groups among this nation who want to live according to your will. This nation has come forth, naked and hungry, with a sad heart longing for you, the Father, and hoping for a new nation and a new promise. Because this nation appeals to you in a naked state, we believe that the bond of heart that cannot abandon this nation is strong, and because this nation appeals to you from a place of suffering and hunger, we know that you regard this nation more highly than any other. 
We bow before you with such a heart, Father. We have nothing. We have nothing to boast about, and we have not prepared any offerings to give you. Although we have a sincere desire to give, we have nothing to offer, and although we have a strong desire to protect your dignity and environment, we are in a position where we cannot do so. 
However, our hearts want to serve you more than anyone else, more than any nation, and more than any believer. We want to serve you, and we want to fight all battles with you under your wing. We are the nation you have called among many nations, and we are your sons and daughters whom you have called among many believers. We dare to hope that you will look favorably upon our hearts and find us. 
We have understood your command to come, and we have understood your intention to push us to pioneer this path many times. When we were discouraged, you encouraged us, and when we were in sorrow, you comforted us by saying, "I am here." We know that you were like this in the past, you are like this now, and you will be like this tomorrow. We know that we cannot connect with you in comfortable places, nor can we meet you on smooth paths. This is because you have not yet been in a comfortable place, and you have not yet walked the smooth path. 
We have learned and realized through experience that only those who try to bear the Father’s sorrow as their own and walk the path of the Father’s suffering can be directly addressed by you and can express their circumstances from a natural heart. We also know that this is the most precious thing. 
Father! Please remember this time especially. Bless countless humans and bless the many denominations that call upon your name among them. Moreover, bless those who hold onto your heart and are being pushed, and bless those who have stepped forward to be offered as heavenly mountain offerings, regardless of blood, sweat, and tears. We believe that you will be with them and fight alongside them. 
Those who follow your lonely path are also lonely people.

The Resolve of the Absolute Being
The absolute being has a resolve as an absolute being that no one can change, which is necessary for the providence of salvation to save this evil world. What kind of resolve is that? How does it treat sinners, and how does it treat good people? It must not change due to anyone's advice or yield to anyone's circumstances until it completes the world of the creation ideology from individuals to families, nations, the world, and ultimately the entire universe. This resolve is unchangeable even after countless eons have passed. The day that presents this resolve to all people is the judgment day spoken of in Christianity. That day is when God's resolve is actually shown before sinful humanity. Today, countless people live on this earth, and many saints exist, but they do not know what God's resolve is. However, God is carrying out the providence of salvation under that unchanging resolve.

Humans must receive historical recognition.
What must we do to stand confidently before the judgment seat? We must receive historical recognition. Because we are historical beings, we must receive historical recognition. Next, we must receive providential recognition. If there is no God, we would not know, but since there is a God who has been providentially dealing with humanity, humans must receive providential recognition from Him. To pave the way for this recognition, religion must emerge in the human world. If any ideology has emerged in history, that ideology must be recognized from a standpoint that can face a world. Therefore, people seek ideologies and ideals. They seek global ideals and cosmic ideals. What does this mean? It means that all humanity living on the earth must create an environment where they can receive historical recognition and enter the world of historical connections as a whole. Thus, they must receive historical recognition.

Then, does receiving only historical recognition solve everything? No. No matter how great a politician or figure one may be on this earth, even if they act according to God's will on behalf of the times and history, they cannot manage the universe that moves around God. Therefore, after receiving historical recognition through a certain standard, one must also receive providential recognition. There is a purpose of heaven that is historically dealing with this earth, and one must receive recognition that can address that purpose. Thus, until now, many saints have abandoned this earth, disregarded this era, and sought to be absorbed into a new era. They have devoted themselves to the providential new era and the providential time.

These individuals have established a certain ideology according to their respective nations and have equipped themselves with a new religious form that can escape the established environment, transitioning through a providential era where they can possess a global religious ideology in today's global ideological age. Just as the world and history have gone through revolutionary paths, religion has also gone through revolutionary paths. Even when looking at today's global ideologies, we see that under the ideals of freedom and equality, they are seeking one world, that is, one sovereign world and one ideological world. This indicates that not only external world movements but also a time must come when a global religious movement will be presented.

Therefore, a time must come when humanity can receive historical recognition and be acknowledged as beings without fault before the entire history. This is the era of hope we desire, the era of hope that history longs for, the ideal era.

The Purpose of Religion
So, does everything end with that? No. On that foundation, we must receive providential recognition. We must establish an era that can represent God and unite with that era. Therefore, we must receive historical recognition and providential recognition.

Then what must come next? Providence is taking direction through the ideology of religion, and when it reaches a certain standard, ultimately, God and humanity must meet. This is precisely what humanity has pursued and what religion has sought until now.

Until now, religion has worked to bring God down and elevate humanity to unite God and humanity. This is the purpose of religion. Religion has lifted fallen humans, those in evil, those who cannot relate to heaven at all.

God! Come down. Humanity! 
Rise up. The purpose of religion is to unite God and humanity as one heart.

The absolute creator has made great efforts to come to find us humans. We must understand this. The creator has worked alone throughout the long course of history to find humanity. Isn't that the logic?

Therefore, you must understand. We are a historical stepping stone. We are a stepping stone. Humans must receive recognition of the heart.
What kind of recognition must come next? After receiving historical recognition and providential recognition, one must receive God's recognition of the heart. Why is that?

Only then can no one break that bond, and they become a perfect father-son relationship. A perfect and exemplary father-son relationship, where there can be no complaints, the father is the father, and the son is the son.

If God has made a providential effort with such resolve toward a world of purpose, what should humanity do? After receiving historical recognition and providential recognition, they must also receive the recognition of God's heart. Then everything will be fine. To do that, one must be able to say, "If you die, I die; if you live, I live." One must rise to the standard where "what is yours is mine, and what is mine is yours." This is not a game that is introduced and played. You must understand this. It is not about Jesus coming and building a bridge. It is direct. The era of receiving recognition of the heart is a direct era. Can recognition of the heart be given indirectly? Can one explain that the heart is like this or that through a trustworthy disciple and expect the heart to connect? It must be direct.

Thus, God is guiding numerous nations on this earth to establish the world of the heart that He desires, while gathering numerous ideologies and movements toward one world. Now, there are only two ideologies closest to one world, and that is the end. Therefore, in today's world, conflicts, breakages, and problems arise. Since the world is like this, religion must also clash. It cannot be resolved as it is. There must be clashes. Those responsible must clash with those responsible, and believers must clash with believers. Through this chaos, a revolution must occur. This is a historical fact. It is a historical fact.

We should not despair in such a complicated environment; we must recognize that this era demands a new resolve from us. We should not despair here and look back but should look forward and move on. We must understand that it is time to make a new resolve instead of remaining stagnant and in a state of giving up.

No sovereign from the past has survived in the course of history. Anyone who has proclaimed any ideology in the past has faded away when the global ideological era has come. Anyone who has claimed any sect in the past could not transition toward the new ideological era. Isn't that right?

Looking at the history of Israel, they went through 4,000 years from Adam and 2,000 years from Abraham, and after countless hardships, they established the chosen people of Israel. God shed tears with that nation and fought with that nation, shedding blood with them. Then, at the end of the 4,000 years after Adam and the 2,000 years after Abraham, when the national prestige crumbled, the social environment blurred, and the religious ideology disappeared, Jesus was born. At that time, the people of Israel were supposed to fulfill their historical mission and advance to a position where they could receive historical and providential recognition, but they could not do so.

For what purpose did Jesus come to this earth? He came to directly connect humanity to God. In other words, He came to find the emotional resolution. In the end, there is no need to worry about sinning and falling. Those are all side issues. If the emotional problem is resolved, there is no need to worry about such things. Therefore, fallen humanity has the responsibility to pour out all their sincerity, to squeeze out their blood and flesh, and to resolve God's emotional sorrow that has penetrated to their bones. This is the most important thing in the providential course.

The Purpose of Jesus Coming to Earth
If the people of Israel had followed the historical environment according to Jesus' will and had become providential representatives, standing victorious before God's emotional judgment seat, the providence of the past 2,000 years would not have been extended. Why? Because what is determined by God's heart and resolved by God's heart cannot be governed by anyone and cannot be turned back by anyone. In that case, even Satan is defeated. Therefore, those who have received grace are the first to know this.

We must connect emotionally with God and experience His heart. Those who have not experienced the emotional connection can never go before the Father. But what about the people of Israel during Jesus' time? They were established with God's tears, established with God's blood, and established with God's sweat; yet, the chosen people of Israel forgot all of that. They completely forgot.

Before such a nation, Jesus appeared rearmed. What was His mission? Was it to take the people of that time and send them to heaven? No. His mission was to resolve the historical tears of God, the historical blood and sweat of God. If He could not fulfill that mission, God's will could not be concluded.

To fulfill this will, a historical nation is absolutely necessary. A nation that can establish an ideological state on behalf of all humanity is needed. On the foundation of that nation, Jesus, while they did not know, shed God's tears, blood, and sweat, which were within their bodies, and taught them and showed them in reality. If they had united with that nation, the hope of the Christian 2,000-year history, the thought of the Second Coming, would not have existed.

So, did Jesus come to this earth for the people of Israel? He came to show them that the chosen nation had lost its historical content, and then He came to fulfill the providential purpose. God, as an incorporeal spirit, shed tears and, as an incorporeal spirit, shed blood and sweat, but He could not show that as a reality before humanity. To show that as a reality and to embrace humanity as a reality, Jesus came as the true Father of humanity.

What we must understand here is that as long as heaven guides the nation with an absolute resolve, the people of Israel, who follow heaven, must unite under that absolute resolve to welcome the Messiah. If they had done so, they would not have become as miserable as they are today. Judaism still remains on this earth. The leaders who captured and killed Jesus, the persecutors, and those who betrayed heaven as instruments of Satan still exist. Therefore, God has not yet avenged His enemies. He has not avenged them.

The Heart of Jesus that Prayed for His Enemies Even in Death
Where was the original heart of Jesus that could pray for His enemies even in death? Jesus thoroughly understood that God was working providentially to completely restore humanity, to restore the world of goodness, and to destroy evil. Even if He had to fall, He knew that there remained a foundation for the battle against evil. When He looked at the people of Israel who were pushing Him toward death, He could not utter words of curse.

It was not about His own life that suffered on this earth; it was about Himself, who had to take responsibility for the entire nation and resolve the historical sorrow, pain, and injustice of God. Knowing that He was the one who had to lead the pitiful people of Israel in the course of history, Jesus could not open His mouth to curse, because He understood that God was the one who had suffered far more than His own agony or bleeding pain. It was not just love that made Him do that; it was the understanding of such a heart.

From Noah to Abraham, Moses followed God's will vaguely without knowing, making resolutions and sacrifices, but knowing God's pain, tears, and injustice, and God's efforts to awaken and gather ignorant humans toward one purpose, Jesus thought that it was not a problem for Him to die. We must feel that heart of Jesus.

How much blood, sweat, and tears did God shed to establish a hopeful nation that could send the Messiah? Jesus thought about what would happen if even these people fell. If Jesus had cursed the people of Israel, saying, "May they be judged and perish," they would have all been destroyed that very day. Those who were blessed would all be subject to judgment. However, even if it meant striking Himself a million times, Jesus prayed for their blessing, and you must clearly understand that heart of Jesus.

The Reason Jesus Walked the Path of Blood, Sweat, and Tears
Throughout His 30 years of life, Jesus shed tears. He shed tears that penetrated to the bone and flesh. Although it is not recorded in the Bible, Jesus lived in deep sorrow. On this earth, filled with sin, many people lived comfortably and joyfully. Yet, Jesus, who should have lived in the glory of glories, lived in tears. Not only tears but also sweat.
Yes. In the end, He shed blood on Golgotha. Not only did He shed tears and sweat for this land, but ultimately He shed blood as well.  
What is that blood? It is the tears that God has shed for 4,000 years since Adam and 2,000 years since Abraham, inherited on behalf of the nation, even if the nation perishes. If we do not inherit those tears, when Israel falls, God's providence will be cut off. Jesus was the one who had to inherit God's tears. Despite the betrayal of the Israelite nation, Jesus was the one who had to inherit the sweat of God, who has labored to lead them until now. Jesus, who appeared in place of history, was the one who had to inherit tears, so He could not help but shed tears.  
Our Resolve  
Many prophets were sacrificed, and blood was shed to lead the Israelite nation out and to welcome Jesus, but if Jesus were to cut off the Israelite nation there, the history of God's tears would be severed. The history of blood would collapse. Therefore, we must clearly understand that Jesus walked the path of shedding blood and the path of death to not destroy the tradition of the blood history that God has labored over for 4,000 years.  
Although the Israelite nation has fallen away, the 4,000 years of history that has been providentially guided toward the Israelite nation, the entangled emotional history through God's heart, has been passed on to those who believe in Jesus today, creating the Second Israel. If Jesus had cursed them and repaid their enmity with enmity, He might have satisfied His own desires, but the historical connection would have been severed. The historical connection would have been cut off. Even if the Israelite nation perishes, the history of sweat, tears, and blood shed for the Israelite nation must not be severed. That was the original intention. The altar that Abel's blood cries out from must not be destroyed.  
The image of Jesus praying with blood and sweat in the Garden of Gethsemane, the holy figure of Jesus carrying the cross toward Golgotha, shows that the Israelite nation became a group of traitors who betrayed heaven, but the sad history of God who labored to establish them has been passed on. We must clearly understand that Christianity is the inheritance of this history of tears, this history of sweat, and this history of blood.  
Those who do not know this content will perish. The Israelite nation perished because they did not know this. You should not just enter and exit the church with the Bible and hymnals; you must know Jesus, who represents the God who sheds blood, the God who sheds tears, and the God who sweats. It is through such sacrifice and death that Christianity's tradition conquers the world, and it is the traditional path by which God comes to find humanity. Any sect or orthodoxy is not an issue.

You have come here, exhausted from being pushed around this way and that. The most sorrowful thing for the person speaking here is that. It is sorrowful.
