The next three years will be a global turning point. If we are late, it may extend to seven years. It is a turning point, a turning point. Now you must find the homeland of your heart. Even if you long for the knees of the mother who gave you birth, it is in vain. You must seek the homeland of your heart, the owner of your heart. We have sought social goodness for 2,000 years, but it has not worked, so we must pursue the goodness of the heart. We must reflect on how good our hearts are here and lament. We must think about how broad and how noble our hearts are, and how much strength we have to live in a valuable form. If that is not the case, we need a collaborator who can develop that, a doctrine or ideology that can awaken our hearts with just one word. Thus, standing on the basis that this is the last and has an irreplaceable value, we must be able to embrace heaven and earth and sleep comfortably in the vast universe. Only by sleeping that sleep and waking up can we become the sons and daughters of the new nation. Only by having such a heart and becoming victors can we become heirs of God. I know this.

So, everyone, do not listen to anyone’s words. Spiritually speaking, this time is becoming increasingly critical. Smart people unknowingly become objects of criticism. The loyalty of friends is nowhere to be found, and everywhere you go, it is only things that hurt your heart. The social foundation you believed in stimulates you. Whether at home or out in society, it is the same. But does that make your heart comfortable? No, it does not. What can we do? It is impossible. No matter how capable you are, no matter how smart you pretend to be, it is of no use.  
Humanity must develop the heart’s field.  
In this age that is approaching the end, you must be able to hear the murmurs of your conscience. If you do not have a place, a nest, an ideological foundation in your life where you can awaken your heart’s murmurs and discern the times and eras to develop your heart’s field, both you and this nation will be pitiful. If our thirty million people can establish such an ideology in this chaotic world, we will dominate the world. The culture of the world, the history of the world, and all sovereignty may disappear, but if that nation becomes indispensable in the new cultural era, that nation can dominate the world. If that nation becomes a nation that must not be absent in the new ideal age, it can dominate the world. If that happens, no sovereignty will be a problem, and even those who boast loudly can be dominated. When it becomes a time when it is okay to be like this or that, or even to die, that will be the end.

Now that the end has come, you must make a new resolve to develop your heart’s field. How should you make a new resolve? You must resolve to go with God, whether it be the path of tears or the path of death. You must transcend life and death.  
That is why when Jesus first set out to proclaim the gospel, he made a solemn resolution. The heart of Jesus, who had to awaken the sleeping Israelite people, was burning. He did not try to awaken their sleep. He intended to tear down the sleeping house. That is Jesus’ mission. He intended to tear down the living house, the temple, and everything. Since they kept sleeping in the house, he thought he should tear down the house first.

The foundation of human life is the heart. It is love. Fallen humans must overturn the love for parents, love for siblings, love between spouses, and love for anyone else. That is why Jesus said, “Anyone who loves their father or mother more than me is not worthy of me; anyone who loves their son or daughter more than me is not worthy of me; and whoever does not take up their cross and follow me is not worthy of me.” (Matthew 10:37-38)  
Thus, Jesus advocated a heart revolution to awaken the sleeping consciences of humanity. Throughout the 4,000 years of history, many ancestors shouted many ideologies, but who ever said to love me more than parents or siblings? Jesus intended to carry out a heart revolution. He faced opposition when he tried to revolutionize what was tangled on the ground, what Satan possessed, with the power of the heart.

Jesus said to his mother, “Woman, why do you involve me?” That is natural. He spoke well. When his mother and brothers came looking for Jesus, he said, “Who is my mother, and who are my brothers? Whoever does the will of my Father in heaven is my brother and sister and mother.” We must honor Jesus by seeing this. This is the first proclamation of Jesus advocating a heart revolution.

The condition to stand closest before God  
Those who hesitate and wander while holding onto the word will not be able to pass the final judgment. Jesus sought to awaken sleeping humans to develop the heart’s field. He must understand that God’s work is to create a nation that will rise from the depths of hell by stripping away the blankets and beating them until their bottoms burn.

In today’s global end times, God’s work will unfold through the most pitiful nation. A country like Korea has many conditions to be blessed. So do not be discouraged. The grateful thing is that God is coming to find such a nation with those conditions. Right now, Korea is divided into North and South, with parents in the North and children in the South, husbands in the South and wives in the North, all longing for each other emotionally. This is God naturally separating hearts. As they struggle through the difficult lives of refugees, they end up fighting and quarreling because they cannot trust each other. Isn’t that so? It is the same for church elders and pastors. From a principled perspective, these things are not bad phenomena.

If the ideological world that Jesus advocated is to come, we know that it will emerge from such a nation. We must love Jesus more than ourselves and love God more than Jesus. Is that not so? As I mentioned earlier, we must receive historical recognition, providential recognition, and recognition of the times.  
What is the condition to stand closest before heaven? It is you yourselves. The older gentlemen and ladies here must have given birth to and raised children. Then have you loved God more than the heart you have for your children, holding them and nursing them? If you have not, that is absolutely unacceptable. Later, that child will appear before the judgment seat and appeal. Did you love God more than your husband? Later, that husband will appeal at the judgment seat.

The path of the way  
The path of the way is a path of sacrifice, a path of letting go. I do not want to say this, but that is the principle. You must let go of even your beloved children. Even if that child is in a pitiful and resentful position, you must leave them behind. Look. God has done such things.  
He sent his beloved child to this earth to be wronged and despised. He allowed the chosen ancestors to face injustice. Was it because He had no love? He loved them, but because they had to become the offering representing the earth, He had to sprinkle the blood of love and the blood of goodness. Thus, He intended to establish families by making individuals offerings, to establish nations by making families offerings, and to establish the world by making nations offerings. He intended to establish the world by making the Israelite nation an offering. You must understand this clearly.

The Israelite nation perished through blood. A nation that causes its beloved nation to perish cannot conquer the world.  
Then what will God make that world face by placing it in such a position? He will make them seek God. Today, the world is being swept into such a quagmire.  
Here, we must make a solemn resolution to develop the heart’s field. You must let go of your beloved sons and daughters before your eyes. God called Noah and told him to believe for 120 years, then pushed him onto the path of rejection and persecution. The same goes for Abraham. God blessed Abraham by saying, “Your descendants will be as numerous as the stars in the sky and the sand on the seashore,” and then told him to leave Ur of the Chaldeans. Likewise, God appeared to Jacob while he was sleeping on a stone pillow on his way to Haran, blessed him, and then sent him to Haran, where he suffered for 21 years. The same goes for Moses. Knowing that the Israelite nation was God’s chosen people and that they must stand before God’s will, God saw Moses’ burning national spirit as he killed the Egyptian who was fighting with his brother, the Israelite, and sent him to the Midian wilderness to suffer for 40 years.

Jesus was the same. He was the heavenly prince sent as the savior of this earth, the only begotten son of God. He was the son of God, the Lord of hosts, and the King of kings. Yet, when such a son was sent to this earth, he was born in a lowly stable. However, Jesus was grateful. He was grateful no matter what. He came empty-handed, so he would leave empty-handed. He came from the heart of the Father, so he would go holding onto the heart of the Father. This was Jesus’ life goal.  
Having been born of the blood and flesh of parents and having received the seed of love, he must carry that with him. Since he was sown from that, if he does not hold onto that, he cannot be registered in the heavenly world. Knowing this, Jesus came to this earth and lived for over 30 years, only to be rejected. He was rejected by his parents. He was pushed away by his nation. He was pushed away by his friends. He was pushed away by his church. In the end, he was even betrayed by the twelve apostles who followed him, and even more so, he was betrayed by his three beloved disciples. Ultimately, did he not say he did not know God?  
“O my Father, why have you forsaken me?” Even in the place where God forsook him, Jesus said, “Even if God forsakes me, the center of this heart that loves you cannot change.” Because of this, Jesus became the one qualified to face all people as the center of the heart that represented God on this earth, even if God left him. You must know this fact.

In today’s age, we must know this ideology and will and awaken a revolution of the heart. Furthermore, we must carry out a revolution of the heart. While communists shout about a revolution of consciousness, we must not do that but propose a revolution of conscience to awaken the conscience and even raise a revolution of the heart. When such movements appear in this universe, the world of Satan will collapse. This means that the foundation of evil will collapse.  
Therefore, you must hold onto your hearts, remove everything that hinders the awakening of your hearts, and organize yourselves under a solemn resolution and determination to cultivate your heart’s field. Thus, I sincerely hope that you will become the owners of hearts who can embrace heaven and earth, restoring the original state before the fall.  
<Prayer> Father! While wandering on a difficult path, I have found an even more difficult path. The way that leads to death is wide and smooth, but the way that leads to life is narrow and rugged.  
Father! I thought it was the end once I went, but there is still a path left to go. I know that there are countless difficulties to resolve all that has been tangled in history for 6,000 years. I long for the day when I can explode with the heart that can overcome all these difficulties and sing while embracing my own self. To achieve this, I must make a new resolution.  
Now I understand that if I do not have this ideology and do not establish that standard, I cannot pioneer the world. I must cultivate my heart’s field, awaken my sleeping heart, look to my original Father, and with both hands joined, while all cells, blood, flesh, and bones move, call upon the Father and shed tears of gratitude and reverence, leading us to a touching place where we can bow our heads in awe.  
I hope and desire that a path, a movement, and a final ideology that cannot be exchanged for anything in this world, and that cannot be betrayed even if it means death, will appear on this earth.  
Knowing that such a movement will surely appear on this earth before the day of judgment, we have come today with the name of unification. We are grateful for being pushed by our nation and do not feel wronged for being persecuted by our social environment.  
Every time that happens, I think about how it becomes the material to cut the historical thread of resentment and break down the barriers of historical sorrow, and I am filled with joy toward that world, toward the humanity I wish to embrace, and toward the new land I wish to settle in, and I have resolved to shed sweat, tears, and blood. Please protect us. Even at this time, there are beloved sons and daughters fighting in such environments, disregarding their blood and flesh. I earnestly hope and desire that you will protect and keep them.
Before awakening the sleeping nation, I must first awaken myself to understand how the nation is asleep and how humanity in the world is asleep. I know that I have a mission to understand and awaken all that is in heaven and on earth, so I ask that I may have a heart that can resonate with the Father's heart and be equipped with the appearance of one who is awakened, so that I can call the Father "Father" and the people of the earth "brothers." Thus, you are indeed the resting place of the gospel where you can dwell forever. I sincerely hope and desire that all who are qualified may be able to do so.

I earnestly ask that these individuals feel deeply that returning to the embrace of the Father with a new determination and a new heart is the most important thing. I pray all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.

You represent heaven and earth and embody the universal position that represents the whole will. Therefore, you must make a resolution and pledge from a responsible position.

After training, you must go out with the position of a leader. You must know yourselves and understand our position.

Know that you are those who have inherited the bloodline of the fall. Remember that you must cleanse the bloodline of the fall and continue a new history. If you feel wronged, angry, and unable to endure while looking at history and reality, you must realize that the bloodline of the fall and the seeds of sin are present in history and reality.

Conquering oneself is the key that determines whether one can achieve results before heaven. Until now, you have cursed and spoken ill, but after knowing this will, you must not do so. You carry the ties of sin. To cut this off, you must be ruthless. The Bible says that if your hand or eye causes you to sin, you should remove it. Only when this is possible do you gain strength.

November 11, 1960 (Friday), Former Headquarters Church.  
* This message was organized from notes taken by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee.

When starting this path, the teacher set the slogan to complete self-governance before governing the universe and began. When walking a path unknown to others, one must endure persecution, misunderstanding, and even weapons. You must have the mental composure to embrace everything and break through the enemy lines.

You must be able to use all your circumstances as materials and teaching materials. When the time comes to be cornered by your environment, you should be grateful. It is God's will to completely occupy you. The most painful thing is losing the position where we can regard God as our Father. This feeling of resentment has existed since our ancestors.

We did not know the true God and the true person. How wonderful it would have been if true individuals and families could transcend society, nations, and the world, and possess public value! If there is something to be resentful about, nothing is more resentful than the fallen state.

Today, people know that evil exists, but they do not realize that they are descendants of the fallen bloodline. They do not know the true God, true parents, true couples, true siblings, true nations, and true worlds. If God wishes to save such people, there must first be a choosing. There must be a selection of individuals, families, nations, and peoples.

In history, there has been the idea of a chosen people, and the chosen nation was Israel, which had the ideology of regarding God as the true Father. The true heaven and earth were within that ideology.

We are resentful, but there is one who is even more resentful, and that is God. Because there is the ideology of the true kingdom of God, to realize that ideology, we must resolve this resentment. To resolve this resentment, there must be a fundamental declaration.

The beginning and the end, the start and the finish can be very close depending on the case. The ends can meet directly.

Even at this moment, God is walking the path of fierce battles. If God is resentful and I am resentful, we must understand the content to resolve this resentment. If something has come out to solve this, how much do you understand its value? How much have you considered the value of the true God, true parents, true family, and true siblings? If not, there is no way to resolve it. When our ancestors fell, they did not know, but after the fall, they felt resentment. If there are any enemies left on the earth, we must subdue them and greet the day of reconciliation.

God's anger cannot be resolved by God Himself. It is anger caused by humanity, so we humans must resolve it. We cannot resolve that anger until we have a heart that is more resentful than God's anger. Today, those who walk this path may have grievances, but they cannot express them because God has not yet resolved His anger.

You must resolve the grievances of the fallen Adam and Eve while alive. Cutting off the line of Satan's operations is the purpose of establishing the path.

You must clearly know who the first enemy and the second enemy are in God's establishment of humanity. The first enemy is Satan, and the second enemy is the wicked humans who betray God.

The first center is God, and the second center is also God. To solve the problems of the end times, a religious form must emerge. The first line must separate and strike the first evil, and the second line must separate and strike the second evil; the day that happens is the day of judgment.

If the first enemy and the second enemy have united, but the first line and the second line cannot unite, they will perish. Evil perishes once, but good differs in that it overcomes evil and revives.

To resolve God's anger, we must recognize that we have become servants of the first enemy and instruments of the second enemy. We must become the embodiment of God's hope and resolve God's anger.

All people on earth are in sorrow. They have lost their original hometown, their original parents and siblings, and everything original. They must not fail to feel this.

Knowing the sorrow caused by the fall, we must resolve it without fail. We must shed many tears. If we shed tears for our nation, our country, or for heaven, we can become corresponding leaders.

When sorrow seeps into a quiet place, the history of revival begins to sprout from there. That place is the place of regeneration. It is the most sacred place. If we hold the nation and the world and shed tears, we can each receive their blessings, and if we hold God and shed tears, we can participate in the place of receiving God's blessings.

There must be such movements on the earth, and thankfully, Christianity is a religion of tears. If there are those who are not joyful even when they eat or wear something, they are religious people. If society, the nation, and the world can mourn for God, they are the protagonists of the world.

Patriots and loyal subjects are all those who have crossed the valley of tears. We must recognize that we are resentful descendants. We cannot be comfortable even when we eat or work. We cannot lift our heads.

Because God has worked harder than us, if you feel sorrow in your heart, you must say, "Beloved Father, please inherit all of Your sorrow to me." If there is someone who inherits the sorrow of world history, the history of heaven will unfold because of them.

For 6,000 years, God has not been able to say, "I am your Father, and you are my children." He has not been able to find such sons and daughters. It has taken 6,000 years to find such sons and daughters. Therefore, we must take responsibility for the sorrowful history. I must cooperate with the good ones to be able to eat and sleep.

We must replace God's sorrowful position. Jesus came as the king of Israel, but he never commanded with the sovereignty of that king. The one who could not exercise power and played the role of a prince of defeat is the sorrowful Jesus.

To become loyal subjects and ultimately to become God's true sons and daughters, we must take on the burden of the hard work that Jesus has done for 2,000 years.

You trainees must discover that you are in a profoundly sorrowful position. You must feel this deeply. You must know that you are in a sorrowful state and that you are the focal point of problem-solving. You must realize that there are enemies who invade your resentful position and become one who bears grievances again.

Having become descendants of a sorrowful history, we must take responsibility for God's grievances and resolve them. We must comfort God, who is grieving in the judgment seat, saying, "Please do not judge this sinful nation." We must have another heart of leisure that can do this. We are loyal subjects and filial sons, so we must ask God to forgive those who are with us when He sees us. Only then can we become those who remain in the new era.

To comfort the resentful God, we must enter into the place of resentment, and to comfort the sorrowful God, we must enter into the place of sorrow. Let us go out to serve the infinitely sorrowful God. Let us go out to comfort the infinitely sorrowful God. Let us go out to resolve the infinitely resentful God's grievances. Only when such sons and daughters arise will the history of sin come to an end.

Do not repay our enemies. God, please repay only the first enemy. We will take responsibility for repaying the second enemy in place of God. This is the judgment of the saints. We must stir up indignation against Satan, but we must know how to pray for the world and humanity.

The purpose of learning the word, the purpose of refining character, and the purpose of equipping the heart is to understand God's heart, to crush Satan, and to be able to bring back those who are on Satan's side. Only then can we enjoy the glory of victory that we have won over Satan.

To create you who bear resentment, sorrow, and grievances, and to make you into heavenly soldiers who can unite and fight until the enemy is defeated is the teacher's purpose.

**"For three years, endure the suffering of death"**

<Summary of the Message> Just as we feel the changes of the times, we must also feel changes in our faith life. Just as there are spring, summer, autumn, and winter in a year, there are cycles like that in a day. In our lifetime, there are also periods similar to spring, summer, autumn, and winter.

Just as these days are the harvest season, historically, this time is the time of harvest. The difference between autumn and summer is that while summer's leaves cover all the blemishes of the tree, when autumn comes and the leaves fall, the true identity of the tree is fully revealed.

This is also true from a providential perspective today. What should you, in this era, be like? Looking at the currents of thought that have appeared in history, there are many blemishes, but we must bear some fruit from them.

Spring and summer exist for the purpose of autumn.

You must become a person who can bear fruit in an unchanging form. No matter how many blemishes a tree has, if it bears fruit, the owner rejoices upon seeing it.

Just as a seed planted goes through winter and sprouts in spring, grows in summer, and brings forth new fruit in autumn, in our faith life, we must also go through a period of trials once again to give birth to new life.

If we are to be historical fruit-bearing entities, we must bear new life forms in this land where blemishes are revealed.

Ancient civilizations are like tropical civilizations, and modern civilizations are like autumnal civilizations. The winds of civilization like winter are the currents of communism.

We must bear fruit from the bare branches from which the leaves have fallen. Now we must sprout new shoots and propagate new life forms.

When the Creator asks, "What kind of valuable existence are you, and what purpose are you aiming for?" what will your answer be?

Will you boast of your environment, boast of lush leaves, or boast of bare fruits or seeds buried in the ground?

Think about what you have lived by as a standard until now.

If you spend your time longing for spring or summer, before you know it, autumn and winter will come. You must go through the winter season to see spring again.

If you have borne fruit, you must go into the ground once. You must go through a period where you are trampled and seem to have no value. At that time, you must not dream of something like spring or summer.

The winter season, which brings great trials, must be felt, and new preparations must be made. That time is the time of judgment.

Just as the fruit of the plants is gathered before the owner, the question is whether you can be gathered before heaven.

To become a fruit-bearing entity, you must have some connection.

Your environment and heart must be aligned before some standard.

The returning Lord comes as a representative fruit-bearing entity that appears in the autumn season.

The owner desires the fruit that he wanted when he planted. However, God has come out with something that has lost its fruit and resembles a dead tree.

The owner will present you as a fruit-bearing entity, but what kind of valuable existence will the owner present you as? What kind of fruit-bearing entity have I become until now? Until now, the bloodlines have been different, the environments have been different, the goals of life have been different, and the forms of fruit have truly varied.

If there is a form of the fruit that heaven desires, what kind of relationship do I have with it, and what state am I in?

Even if I have something to boast about in spring or summer, the fruit is what gathers all the sap and essence.

Both the appearance of adverse conditions and the appearance of favorable conditions manifest in a complete form.

You must not loosen your heart. You must absorb all environmental factors. What kind of existence will you become? Will you become a fruit that can be praised when it appears before the Absolute Being, a fruit that is set aside, or a fruit that must be discarded because it is useless?

If it has not become a fruit of hope, it must die, but to avoid that, it is necessary to cut off the past and graft onto a perfect branch to obtain good fruit; this is the providence of heaven.

If you have borne fruit, you should pick the fruit and plant it in the ground, but if you have not, you should at least graft it onto a good branch. Heaven's original purpose was not grafting. However, now that it is not possible, how grateful it is to be trying to graft onto a perfect branch.

Now, among the seeds that have been passed down until now, all the bad ones must be cut off. You must be grateful for being cut off.

The trainees have lived according to their own whims until now, but from now on, they must cut off the wrong branches and graft new ones. They must have new hopes.

If you want to become a fruit-bearing entity, you must go through the winter season. This era is the time of harvest and the time of bearing fruit.

When the winter season comes, the north wind and snow strike. In such circumstances, you must silently bury yourself in the ground and propagate new life.

If you do not bear fruit, you must be cut off. Jesus cursed the fig tree that bore no fruit. He showed the appearance of the end times.

In the end times, you must be cut off and grafted onto new branches.

New trainees will know that the time is late. Even if it is late, it is terribly late. You must be cut off to bear the second fruit.

You must become one who can be cut off so that heaven can graft you as it pleases.

If you feel that you are a fruit-bearing entity, you must be prepared to face the winter season. Facing the winter season is not just for individuals; it is also historical and comprehensive.

A worm-eaten seed was planted in the Garden of Eden. The providential history of 6,000 years is to gather this again as a complete fruit.

Will I be the one to be stamped or the one to be gathered? To be stamped is to be in a position of denial. Before the winter season of gathering, I must rot. What rots is the flesh, so the body must suffer.

You must fight and overcome with the resolve to endure death for three years. It is difficult for those who have been around for a long time, that is, those who have been around for more than four years. It is even more difficult for those who have been around for seven years. Those who have been around for five or six years will have their old emotions revived. They will feel irritated.
Old people are easy to fall. They are easy to fall to the ground like seedless fruit. The shape is the same, but there is nothing inside.
To become a fruit-bearing entity, one must go through the cold wind. This is because a fruit-bearing entity must gather and organize everything.
When one cannot remain as a seed, the master comes to pick it or it must fall by itself.
What state are you in now? You may seem to be asleep now, but as long as there is life, there will come a time when you can demonstrate your value. Such a person has no problem wherever they go. Moreover, what you have longed for until now was to bear fruit as a blessed being (Tree of Life, Tree of Knowledge of Good and Evil). The master has anticipated this, but it is disappointing when it does not happen.
Do not spend this autumn season with discouragement. Now is the time to bear fruit.
You must become one who can take root and live wherever the master plants this seed. Those who cannot do so will be cut off. It is not a matter of selectively cutting branches; they will be cut off in chunks.
Based on conscience, a new sprout of life will emerge. It is time for you to be busy. It is not the time for criticism. When you stand before the judgment seat, know that your desire is such, so please entrust it to me. You must become a fruit-bearing entity that can do so.
Pray specially for the evangelists who have gone to foreign lands. Let them endure three years of extreme hardship.
There must be someone who puts in their heart and effort.
The members of the headquarters should know that they are the core and that they have a historical responsibility. When looking to the east, do so for the members in the east, and do the same for the west, north, and south.
For three years, I intend to present such tasks not only domestically but also internationally.
When you pray, the other party will appear.
(After reading a letter from a member in America, he continued speaking)
The only way to gain face with foreigners is through hardship. For three years, one must endure extreme suffering. You will understand when the time comes. Otherwise, you will not have face even for your descendants. Those who do not move for three years will regret it immensely and will fall far behind.
Those who have just entered should be sent to areas that were still empty during the last evangelism and endure any hardship. The members who entered earlier are also different from before.
You should not just attend worship. If you do not start now, there will be no time. The teacher must act now. You should establish the conditions to start and act while the teacher is present.
The teacher knows the time, which is why he does this. In three years, history will unfold, and if your name is there, many people will commemorate it and pilgrimage there barefoot.
Now is an important time to establish tradition. Old people will gradually lose face. Do this while pushing and pulling as you are now. Even if your skills and experience are shallow, if your loyalty is the same as that of the old, the same effect will occur.
Even if I want to command America now, I do not do so because of you. I do not do it because of the poor Korean people.
Faith's Fruit
Hebrews 11:17-40
<Prayer> Father! At this time, please allow us to open the altar of tears that you shed on the historical path, and allow us to open the altar of the sweat that you shed.
We understand that humans living on this sinful land are destined to seek tradition. This land has become one where no one can be trusted. Even beloved children, beloved spouses, and beloved parents cannot be trusted. No matter how much we reach out to trust someone, there is no one to hold our hand, and it has become a desolate and lonely land where we cannot help but feel emptiness and loneliness. Therefore, we infinitely thank you for your profound love behind finding one Father who is not like that before humanity, hosting one bridegroom, and entrusting one son.
Today, we come with empty hands, hoping to resemble your heart with empty hearts, and we have come out hoping to embrace your will with empty chests, having abandoned everything in the world, so please manifest yourself. We are bodies struggling in lonely places without anything to believe in or rely on like children, but we kneel at this time to believe in you, rely on you, and rejoice with you, so please manifest yourself and allow the ignorant to feel you, and let those who know be able to make a new resolution before you at this time, dear Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.
In this age, there is no one calling to run towards the path of original nature. Therefore, Father, please raise your sons and daughters here to fulfill such a mission and enable them to fight in the name of heaven on all the terrible battlefields. Thus, may they become sons and daughters whom you can trust, whom you can love, and whom you can protect, we earnestly hope and wish for this, so please take charge of us and lead us.
We have received the command to come personally, and we have come to this place today, knowing that you have labored more than we have to reach this point. You comforted us when we were discouraged, held us up when we were about to fall, and appeared to comfort us when we cried alone. I believe that your sons and daughters who are prostrated here today are also feeling such heavenly feelings, so let the experiential fact of recognizing your existence with that heart permeate their bones, blood, and flesh. <Message> ... We cannot deny that we are a process-oriented existence moving toward one fruit, one goal. If there is a purpose and content that heaven requires, what could that purpose and content be? It would be a world where faith, which God likes and which all of humanity can like beyond national feelings, bears fruit.
God and humans pursuing fruit
If God has a purpose, the process of historical development will also move toward a world of that purpose. Therefore, the purpose of God's faith and the hope that humanity desires in the historical process must coincide, and that day must surely appear in history when both God and humanity can rejoice. Otherwise, there can be no happiness or joy.
No matter how well one practices faith on this earth and lives with God, if a fruit-bearing entity that can be revered by the whole world and heaven does not appear, God becomes a blind being. If God were such a being, there would be no need for humans to long for Him as the subject of hope.
We can infer the future of history by observing social phenomena. If this history is undoubtedly moving toward a world of some purpose, then at the end of time, some fruit-bearing entity that can discuss ultimate values must appear.
Therefore, humans pursue fruit. If one has lived a day, they must reap the fruit of that day, and if they have lived a year, they must reap the fruit of that year. You cannot deny that you weigh everything in your life, including words and actions, while pursuing fruit. If you bear fruit here, it concludes in good, but if you have made every effort and given your all but do not bear fruit, it concludes in evil.
The same is true in our social life today. If there is something valuable in our hearts that can cause a new awareness and a new force of action, it can bear good fruit, but if today you recognize it as a valuable fruit and like it, but tomorrow you may regret and be discouraged, then it bears evil fruit.
From this perspective, when we reflect on the entire history of humanity, it has been a history of regret after the fact. No matter how complete something may have appeared in the historical process, it cannot be called a historically perfect fruit-bearing entity. Therefore, we must understand that we are still in a state of inadequacy, rushing toward the world of fruit.
Students studying in school also desire some fruit. We cannot deny that we want to connect the value of fruit beyond national and global dimensions to heaven.

It is neither any organization on this earth nor any group. The center of that purpose is precisely ourselves. Moses, chosen as the representative for the inheritance of the national legacy. When the nation of Israel had suffered for 400 years in Egypt and 600,000 people were in distress, heaven, which had established the standard of blessing for the inheritance of family legacy from individuals, had to elevate to establish a representative for the inheritance of national legacy. Even in the path of hardship in Egypt, amidst the persecution of enemies, Moses maintained his integrity and did not forget the idea of being a chosen people. He did not forget the blessings of Abraham and Jacob's house, and he steadfastly cultivated the heart to inherit the national legacy. For Moses, blessings were a natural outcome. Although Moses was in the luxurious palace of Pharaoh as the son of a princess, he had a different motive. Even in such a life, he prayed secretly towards his homeland in the east. Every time he wore fine clothes, he was concerned about the nation that was falling into despair. The more he looked at the nation while wearing fine clothes, the more his heart ached.

He thought, "I would rather not be in this position, but be in the same position as you and wear the same clothes." Every time he looked at them from the luxurious environment he was in, his heart was pierced. He prayed for decades, saying, "God! I will stand at the forefront for that poor nation." He prayed with a single heart, a prayer that could resonate with God's heart. Because of such motives, God chose Moses. Even in a free, rich, and luxurious environment, he devoted himself to heaven and had an unparalleled heart of loyalty for the nation suffering under 400 years of oppression.

Thus, God labored for 2,000 years to find an individual to represent heaven and for 120 years to find a family, and then another 400 years to establish Moses, totaling 2,400 years. Knowing God's heart, which had been filled with such pain, Moses lamented, "Why has the nation You blessed come to this?" He felt the nation's sorrow as his own, the nation's pain as his own, and the nation's injustice as his own, which led him to strike down an Egyptian. This act was not merely about killing a man, but from the emotional aspect of loving his nation. He felt the same sorrow as God, questioning why the chosen nation was in such a position. Because he had the same heart as God, even when he killed the Egyptian, Satan could not accuse him. It was for the sake of the nation and for God.

Not only that, but he realized that his environment was not free and immediately abandoned the luxurious environment. He forsook all his circumstances and dedicated his entire life to the nation for 40 years. He thought, "Shall I return to the palace and defile myself?" and set out towards the Midian wilderness. His steps were accompanied by God. When he turned his back on the nation and the palace to head towards the Midian wilderness, tears blurred his vision. His emotional connection with God was that deep. Thus, he lived as a shepherd for 40 years. If Moses, who walked such a path for the beloved nation with a thorough idea of the chosen people, had lamented his own miserable state, he would have lamented countless times. It was not just for one or two years, but for 40 years. The nation of Israel, which was to inherit the national legacy through Moses, knew that God had heard Moses' tears and heartfelt pleas over 40 years. How could Jesus, who came as the Savior of Israel, be tried in Pilate's court? This was a mistake of the nation. They were afraid that a riot would break out if they killed Jesus. If the Israelite nation had united with Jesus, they could not have killed him.

From the day Jesus came, the Israelite nation should have united around Jesus, who appeared as the embodiment of the temple, the one who would inherit God's legacy after 4,000 years. Jesus appeared as the house of the nation that could embrace all of Israel. From the day He was blessed, from the day He was sent to this earth, He was established as the central representative of the heavenly legacy, and thus cannot be exchanged for anyone. Even if they forsake millions of Israelites, they cannot forsake Jesus.

However, Jesus died. The one who came as the center to be our eternal house on this earth died. After His death, no matter how much the Pharisees and Judaism tried to keep the temple, God could not dwell there, so it was broken. Jesus, who gathered everything and blessed it, is a global representative, so when He falls, everything breaks apart.

However, there was a group that arose as enemies against the chosen nation, holding onto the heart that believed and devoted themselves to the will of the dying Jesus. That group was the followers of Jesus of Nazareth. These people were driven out by the nation and chased by the Roman Empire, and as a group fleeing to death, they expanded globally, becoming Christianity. We must understand that today's Christianity carries the ideology of Jesus and bears the grief of the lost Israel.

Because the first Israel was lost, the ideology of Jesus, who sought to restore the world through Israel, was not fulfilled. Therefore, the history of Christianity has developed by blessing the second Israel to unite with Jesus and carry out the movement to establish a global Israel. The Israelite nation had 12 tribes and 70 elders, and they had to obey Moses' commands. Today, there may be many denominations spread across the world, but they all must obey Jesus.

Just as the twelve sons of Jacob followed Jacob, and the twelve tribes of Moses obeyed Moses, all the many denominations spread across the world today must obey Jesus. What kind of obedience? The sons and daughters of Jacob had to obey Jacob, who obeyed the will, whether they lived or died. In the journey of returning to Canaan, the Israelite nation had to follow Moses, whether they lived or died. Today, all Christians on this earth should not be concerned about their denominations. They must march toward the completion of the global return to Canaan and the establishment of the heavenly kingdom on earth.

This land is like Pharaoh's kingdom. It is the world of Satan. For 6,000 years, this land has been a stepping stone for Satan, and Christians living in this land have walked the path of death. By risking death and fighting, the stepping stone of Jesus has expanded globally. That is why Christianity has entered the realm of authority to dominate more than half of the world. Now we must crush the world of Satan. Do you know why God has remained silent until now? It is because the foundation has been cut off.

Now the time has come for the heavenly command to be given, and Christians spread across the world must transcend denominations and prepare the direction of the second Israel along with the sound of the Lord's trumpet, marching toward the new Eden, the new land of Canaan, and the new heavenly Canaan. Here, denomination is not an issue. My denomination or your denomination is not an issue. The time is now the wilderness era. The 40 years after World War I correspond to the time of the wilderness journey.

During the first, second, and third 40-year periods, the world will be turned upside down. More specific details will be discussed at another time. The world is in a state of distress. Here, no denomination or tribe is an issue. The 70 elders who followed Moses and the Israelite nation walked such a path. Therefore, in the end times, the second Israel must also walk this path. There is a three-year period of hardship to cross the Jordan River and enter the new heaven and new land of Canaan. Just as there was a three-day period of sanctification, Jesus also had a three-day period of suffering on the cross to go to the heavenly garden, and Jacob had a three-day period, and Moses also had a three-day period. Therefore, the Messiah, who comes as the substantial being to inherit the global legacy, must also have such a period, and the descendants of Israel and all Christians worldwide must go through such a journey. 

Only by going through this journey can we hear the trumpet sound of the end that will welcome the ideological world of Canaan.

What will we do here? We must leave without fail. God commanded Abraham, and He commanded Jacob. Jesus also came to lead the nation and complete the mission of restoring the global legacy, but He left without completing that mission, so He must come again.

Now, what kind of mindset should we have? Our purpose is Jesus. The purpose of the Israelite nation that followed Moses was Moses. At the same time, they must hold onto Jesus as the stepping stone. Shouldn't it be so? That is the national mission. Then, in this era, if the Lord is coming, we must welcome the Lord, who comes as the responsible figure to complete the global return to Canaan, and absolutely obey Him. After that, we must go forward to the position where God can command us.

What will you do after you meet the coming Lord? The purpose of meeting the Lord is to prepare to receive the heavenly blessing as the bride and groom. Do you think everything will be fine just by meeting the Lord? Absolutely not! After meeting the Lord, we must accompany Him as the bride and groom and ask God to give us the blessing that He could not give to Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. We must be able to do this. 

We must inherit the global legacy.

Then, what should we do to welcome the Lord who comes at the end? We must welcome the coming Lord and hold onto God. Why? The coming Lord comes because of the earth. Originally, humans lived on the earth, so everything must be resolved on the earth. After that, the destination is heaven. Since humans fell on the earth, everything must be resolved on the earth. Only by completely resolving everything on the earth can we establish heaven, but the Lord went to the spirit world without resolving this, so He must come again. Therefore, the coming Lord is coming to the earth. The Bible says, "Whatever you bind on earth will be bound in heaven, and whatever you loose on earth will be loosed in heaven" (Matthew 16:19). Since they were bound due to mistakes on earth, He comes to completely unbind them on earth. Now is the time to welcome such a Lord, and we must hold onto God through Him.

"God, You are my Father." We must say this. Only by being based on God can we inherit all the legacies of heaven and earth. This is not a public opinion; it is a fact.

Today, there is an enemy confronting Christianity worldwide, and that is communism. What should we do in this situation? Since the time is like this, what should we do?

Let us reflect on the historical Abraham, the historical Jacob, the historical Moses, and the historical Jesus. Of course, they were central figures of their times. What did they have to do? They had to take the land back from Satan and expel Satan from the spirit world so that heaven and earth would belong to the Father. Only then can the will of heaven be fulfilled, but that work has not yet been resolved. When that time comes, "Abraham, what do you have to boast about? Have you prepared to inherit the legacy of heaven and earth?" will be the judgment. In the end, Abraham, Jacob, Moses, and all will be judged in the spirit world. They will be judged because they did not fulfill their responsibilities. The standard for receiving blessings, if Israel is at the national standard, must be connected to the emotional standard that is the goal of the legacy, but it is not so. In the end, we must...
I do not know whether to judge Abraham or the angels. In 1 Corinthians 6:3, there is such authority. If we are the sons and daughters who inherit the estate, we are victors in both the heavenly and earthly realms. To achieve that, everything must be grafted. It is like a side branch sprouting from the root. A single sprout comes out and becomes a new tree. Knowing that this is the end time, you must inherit God's estate today, as the title of today's message suggests.

So what kind of time is the new coming time? The time when God called and established Abraham has passed, the time when He blessed Jacob's family has passed, the time when He called and blessed Moses as the representative of the nation has passed, and the time when He sent Jesus to bless the world has also passed. What era are we in now? It is the time to welcome the returning Lord and to directly approach God and call Him my God.

No matter how many blessings from heaven and earth you have received, you cannot deny God. It will lead to ruin. This is the time we are in.

What can we hold onto to grasp God? It is sincerity. Now that there is freedom of faith, there is no persecution. Even if one wants to be martyred, they cannot. Who would hang themselves for saying something heretical? The democracy that allows for freedom of the press, assembly, and faith has been established for the sake of the end times. Everything that has been made to allow for free faith has a purpose. In our time, no matter how much we toil for heaven and offer our necks in loyalty, we do not face persecution. That time has passed.

So what must we possess? We must have heart. We must have the historical heart of God. God is not a God of the times but a God of history. He is the historical God who has raised many prophets and worked hard throughout the historical process. He has led many people along the path of persecution and martyrdom to bring us to this day to save you. Therefore, He is the historical God.

The prophets of the past did not know. Abraham did not know the historical heart of God who has worked for 2,000 years. Jacob did not know, and Moses did not know. They did not understand how it came to be. They did not know the historical God. Jesus also left without being able to say everything. So what should we do at this time? The age of persecution has passed, and the time for martyrdom has also passed. We must know the historical God. We must know the heart of the historical God. We cannot understand it just by looking at the Bible. That is why, in the end times, we are told to anoint our heads with oil and go into the secret place to pray.

We must pray, saying, "God, what on earth has happened?" 

We must understand the historical heart of God, the heart of the times, and the heart for the future. We must know why God has fought for 6,000 years, why the reality is as it is, and how the future will unfold. Today, Christians scattered throughout the world, the second Israel, must transition to the third Israel. Those who are here today may be hearing this for the first time. We must move toward the ideology of sovereignty of the third Israel. There, our original God is present, our original parents are there, our original spouse and children are there, and there is our original nation, our original country, and our original world. That place is our original heaven and earth, where we can embrace and dance joyfully. No matter how great you are, have you met the original God? You can meet the God who has shed blood and sweat throughout the historical process, and you can meet Jesus who bled on the cross, but you have not met Jesus who leads heaven and earth in the glorious splendor surrounded by countless angels.

Now that the end time has come, we must know what heaven is like. The time of simply believing has passed. Everyone has believed. For 2,000 years, or even 6,000 years, they have believed without resolving anything, so how long will they continue to believe? Therefore, we must know based on the foundation of our belief. What must we know? We must clearly understand the heart of the historical God. We must know how God truly loves me and how He treats the nation.

The God of historical heart has been sorrowful. He has been sorrowful for 6,000 years. He has felt wronged by our unbelieving ancestors. Now we must pray to comfort the God who is sorrowful and wronged. God's heart toward the second Israel scattered throughout the world is filled with sadness. When we hold onto the hem of the Father's garment and say, "Father, why is Your heart so distressed and wronged?" He will hold our hands and say, "Oh, my son, my daughter." 

When Mary Magdalene met the resurrected Lord and wanted to embrace Him, Jesus refused. What must have been the heavenly heart that blocked Him from praising her, saying, "My daughter, how hard you have worked," when He appeared before Mary Magdalene who had searched for Him all night? You must become greater than Mary Magdalene to be called the bride of the Lord. In the current environment, even if you claim to be a bride with the heart you have now, Satan will immediately accuse you.

The Israelite nation that lost the essence of the heavenly inheritance must repent. Today, there are countless people and nations in this world, but there is no group that truly comforts God. If there is a nation that repents on behalf of our ancestors to comfort the historical heart of God, that nation will dominate the world. Father! You have had an indescribably painful heart and sorrowful heart since the time of Adam's family, and through Noah and Abraham, for 6,000 years, You have had an indescribably painful and sorrowful heart. It is sad. Father of history, please forgive me for not being able to serve You as our ancestors did.

The last historical prince of repentance must emerge. Jesus prayed for this for over 30 years. After he had the essence of heart that could inherit the historical estate of God for 4,000 years, he appeared as the Messiah. Is that not so? If not, I believe we cannot call Him the God of love.

Love flows from the motive of relationships through the process and purpose of relationships. It is not blind. Even the children of enemies should be able to say, "Ah, I was wrong," and be loved emotionally. Only then can we approach the eternal God of love.

To send a prince of God who can comfort that wounded heart, God has established a nation through countless hardships for 4,000 years and sent Him to this earth as the essence of the heavenly inheritance, representing the nation of Israel. Yet, the Israelite nation betrayed that essence. In Him are intertwined the 4,000 years of God's heart, the circumstances of 2,000 years ago, and even the future phenomena that can either fulfill or fail God's will, which they did not understand.

The Israelite nation should have cherished Jesus more than anyone in history. Even though there are countless humans, they should have set Jesus above all else, saying He is the best. Because they could not cherish Jesus, who was the best in the past, present, and future, they lost the past Jesus, the present Jesus, and the future Jesus.

We must become sons and daughters who can share joy and sorrow with God. In these end times, you must understand that there must be a nation that is determined to inherit the heavenly inheritance at all costs. God is not a blind God. When you pray, you must hold onto the historical God and repent for the sins of your historical ancestors, shedding tears along with God's tears. Many people have lived and died for 6,000 years for the will, but they did not reach the heart of God to wash away His tears.

In this end time, when we pray holding onto the historical God, we must understand the heart of God that our ancestors did not know, which has passed down through thousands of years since the Adam family. 

You have gone through this and that historical process. 

With a sad heart, we must become friends of God, become His sons and daughters, and become His servants, saying, "Your heart is sad, so my heart is also sad." There has been no one who has done this. A son or daughter of God must emerge who can relieve the sorrow of God, who has historically shed tears and blood and sweat. Not only that, but when we say, "Father! What should we do now?" God should be able to respond, "When you shed tears, I shed tears too. Even if I leave this place, I am yours." A son must emerge who can say this. The Father who was sad in the past and shed tears must be made happy, and I must take responsibility for the sorrowful heart of the Father who could not relieve His sorrow for this age, saying, "I will take responsibility for this age, and I will take responsibility for the enemies of this age, so Father, rest assured."

Thus, a son or daughter must emerge who can hear God say, "The earth is your earth, and the heavens are your heavens. Heaven and earth are all yours, and I, who created this, am yours." A son or daughter must emerge who can bless eternally and completely conclude the emotional foundation that spans the past, present, and future, making Satan, who has accused God for 6,000 years, feel ashamed and unable to raise accusations.

When you shed tears of repentance holding onto the historical heart, God will appear and hold your hand to comfort you. When you shed tears holding onto the heart of the times, you must receive the comfort that God gives. God should be able to say, "When you shed tears, I shed tears; when you smile, I smile; when you suffer injustice, I suffer injustice." You must have a victorious standard that can turn into a unified emotional state, where heaven is your father and you are His son. The standard of blessing must be established on this earth.

That is the hurdle we must overcome. We must move forward until that happens. Then you will be able to act without problem in place of Abraham, who was set as the subject of personal inheritance in the past, without problem in place of Jacob, without problem in place of Moses, and without problem in place of Jesus. Even if it means losing your life, you must do it. You all must do this.

What will the Lord who is coming teach us? He will teach the historical heart of God to the ignorant people of this earth. He will teach the heart of the times and the heart for the future. If you shed tears while holding onto the Lord who is coming, having experienced the sorrows of 6,000 years, that will be the standard by which you can be restored to heaven, having shed tears for heaven. Until now, you did not know this content. Therefore, you must prepare your hearts. Our ancestors betrayed God infinitely on personal, familial, and national levels, even killing Jesus, but we must firmly resolve not to become a tribe of betrayal before the coming Lord. We must vow not to become historical betrayers.

What time is it now? It is a global time. You must not love yourself more than your family. You must not love your family more than society, nor love society more than the nation. You must not love your country more than the world. Now is the time to transition to a global era. We have passed the era of economic warfare and are now in the era of spiritual warfare. We have moved from fighting to seize material possessions to fighting to seize people. Is that not so? We are now fighting to seize people after fighting to seize material and land. The next battle will be to seize God. We are entering the era of religious conflict. This period of religious struggle is a time of confusion. Spiritual phenomena will clash. No matter how capable one may be, there will be no way to resolve it. Even if you try to drive out Satan in the name of Jesus, he will not flee. It is a time when Satan will not run away. When we enter that time, we will be in the global sovereignty era, and when we move into the universal era where heaven and earth are unified, we must not go back.

In this time of transition to such an era, you must shed tears. You must sweat and bleed. You must pray for this nation more than for yourself, and for this world more than for yourself. Today, we have prayed only for the earth. But now, we must not only pray for this earth but also for the spirits in the spiritual world. The spirits in the heavenly world have received permission but have not received blessings, so unless we on earth bless them, they cannot receive blessings. Those spirits in the heavenly world are pitiful. They are looking at the earth. In this age, both the earth and heaven are ours, and all humanity on earth and the countless saints in heaven are also ours. Therefore, the Lord who is coming will be a house that can embrace heaven and earth, and even God.

We must conclude everything with the standard that can embrace heaven and earth. Look at yourselves. Do you know God? You do not. Is there a true ancestor of humanity that God sought to establish? There is none. Without a true ancestor of humanity, there is no true family, and without a true family, there are no true siblings, and without true siblings, there are no true tribes, true nations, or true sovereignty. Is there? There is none.

You are a fallen race. You did not know what kind of being God is. You did not know what a true family, true society, true nation, and true sovereignty are. So what must you do from now on? We must know the glorious God, not the God who has shed countless tears and fought against Satan for 6,000 years. We must know the glorious Jesus and the Holy Spirit, not the one who has fought for 2,000 years. We must know the countless saints who live in glory, not the ones who suffer persecution and pain on earth. Have you seen such saints? You probably have not. Abraham, Jacob, Moses, and Jesus all came to introduce the glorious God and died. They worked hard to introduce the glorious true parents and the glorious true sons and daughters, and to create the glorious true people and true nations. Do you have the confidence to become such a person? Have you seen such people? Have you hosted them?

Heavenly inheritance is given to you on this earth, along with heaven, earth, and God, and at the same time, the lost true parents will be given. What will you do with the lost God, the lost heaven, and the lost earth? God will give you the lost true parents whom He can bless.
What will you do with the True Parents? They will give you True Siblings. By giving True Siblings, they will give you True Tribes; by giving True Tribes, they will give you True Nations; by giving True Nations, they will give you a True World; and by giving a True World, they will create a True Heaven and Earth. Do you understand that, everyone? There is one legacy that will remain on this earth. It is good to receive the earth, and it is good to receive the heavens, but you must become a people of a nation that can embrace the world and love it, based on the emotional connection and direct lineage. Do you understand that now?

What is the final condition to inherit God's legacy? You must have God, True Parents, True Siblings, True People, True Nation, and True World. All of humanity must be my siblings, and you and I must be able to say that we are eternal and unchanging, living as members of a heavenly family through the heart of indissoluble brotherhood. This land is ours, the heavens are ours, and we can say that the Father is our Father. You must become those who can establish a true nation on this earth centered around a true family and inherit the legacy of heaven.

Look, everyone. To establish the Israelite nation, the angels of the heavenly world came and worked. Servants came and worked. Then, the Son came and worked. Now, the Father is coming. The Lord who is coming will come as the Father. He will come as the True Parents and embrace and love the True Children. What will happen then? He will spend the night holding onto each one of you. God loved Abraham more than all of fallen humanity, loved Moses more than all of humanity, and loved Jesus more than all of humanity. Therefore, you must understand how precious each one of you is as a son or daughter loved by God. (The following is omitted due to the recording being stopped.)
